Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Make six sentences using the parts of sentences from each column of the table below:


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
3. Matching:

(a) 'Pahela Boishakh' is the first day of Bangla New Year. ('পহেলা বৈশাখ' বাংলা নববর্ষের প্রথম দিন।)

(b) People from all walks of life celebrate the day with traditional festivities. (সর্বস্তরের মানুষ ঐতিহ্যবাহী উৎসবের মধ্য দিয়ে দিনটি উদযাপন করে।)

(c) The day inspires people to start life with renewed hopes and aspirations. (দিনটি মানুষকে নতুন করে আশা ও আকাঙ্খা নিয়ে জীবন শুরু করতে অনুপ্রাণিত করে।)

(d) People wake up early in the morning to enjoy the day wearing traditional clothes. (লোকেরা ঐতিহ্যবাহী পোশাক পরে দিনটি উপভোগ করার জন্য সকালে ঘুম থেকে উঠে।)

(e) The cultural programme begins just at sunrise. (সাংস্কৃতিক অনুষ্ঠান সূর্যোদয়ের সাথে সাথে শুরু হয়।)

(f) The renowned artists of the country take part in the programme to inspire the participants. (অংশগ্রহণকারীদের অনুপ্রাণিত করার জন্য দেশের স্বনামধন্য শিল্পীরা অনুষ্ঠানে অংশ নেন।)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: প্রতিটি সঠিক বাক্যে প্রথম কলামের বিষয়, দ্বিতীয় কলামের ক্রিয়া/ক্রিয়া-বাক্যাংশ এবং তৃতীয় কলামের অবশিষ্ট অংশ মিলিয়ে এক পূর্ণ অর্থবহ বাক্য গঠিত হয়েছে; এতে বিষয় ও ক্রিয়ার মধ্যে সম্মতি বজায় থাকে ও বাক্যটি পাঠকবুদ্ধিতে অর্থ পৌঁছায়। বাক্যের زمان (tense) এবং ক্রিয়ার রূপ একসাথে রাখা প্রয়োজন যাতে বাক্য গ্রামাটিক্যালি ও লজিক্যালি সঠিক হয়।

Question #2 (ID: 481773)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Make six sentences using the parts of sentences from each column of the table below:

$\begin{array}{|l|l|l|}\hline \text { (a) Wildlife } & \text { (i) is } & \text { (i) on wildlife. } \\\hline \text { (b) Balance of ecosystem largely } & \text { (ii) refers } & \text { (ii) harmful to wildlife. } \\\hline \text { (c) Any development } & \text { (iii) depends } & \begin{array}{l}\text { (iii) to all animals, plants } \\\text { found in the forests. }\end{array} \\\hline \begin{array}{l}\text { (d) Urbanization and } \\\text { industrialization }\end{array} & \text { (iv) should take } & \text { (iv) be extinct. } \\\hline \text { (e) As a result, many animals } & \text { (v) have also increased } & \begin{array}{l}\text { (v) united efforts to protect } \\\text { wildlife. }\end{array} \\\hline \text { (f) For our own existence, we } & \text { (vi) are going to } & \begin{array}{l}\text { (vi) deforestation to a great } \\\text { extent. }\end{array} \\\hline\end{array}$

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Matching:

(a+ii+iii) = Wildlife refers to all animals, plants found in the forests. (বন্যপ্রাণী বলতে বনে পাওয়া সমস্ত প্রাণী, উদ্ভিদকে বোঝায়।)

(b+iii+i) = Balance of ecosystem largely depends on wildlife. (বাস্তুতন্ত্রের ভারসাম্য অনেকাংশে বন্যপ্রাণীর উপর নির্ভর করে।)

(c+i+ii) = Any development is harmful to wildlife. (যেকোনো উন্নয়ন বন্যপ্রাণীর জন্য ক্ষতিকর।)

(d+v+vi) = Urbanization and industrialization have also increased deforestation to a great extent. (নগরায়ণ এবং শিল্পায়নও বন উজাড়কে ব্যাপক মাত্রায় বাড়িয়ে দিয়েছে।)

(e+vi+iv) = As a result, many animals are going to be extinct. (ফলস্বরূপ, অনেক প্রাণী বিলুপ্ত হতে চলেছে।)

(f+iv+v) = For our own existence, we should take united efforts to protect wildlife. (আমাদের নিজেদের অস্তিত্বের জন্য, বন্যপ্রাণী রক্ষার জন্য আমাদের সম্মিলিত প্রচেষ্টা নেওয়া উচিত।)

Explanation:
Explanation: Each sentence is made by combining a subject from the left column, an appropriate verb from the middle column, and a complement from the right column so that both grammar and meaning fit (subject–verb agreement and correct verb collocation). For example, "Wildlife refers to all animals, plants found in the forests" uses "refers to" to define the subject; "Balance of ecosystem largely depends on wildlife" uses "depends on" with "on wildlife"; and "Urbanization and industrialization have also increased deforestation to a great extent" uses a plural subject with "have also increased" taking "deforestation…" as its object. This matching ensures each sentence is grammatically correct and semantically logical.

Question #3 (ID: 481774)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Change the sentences according to the directions:

(a) Newspaper is one of the most useful sources of knowledge. (Positive)

(b) It carries both local and international news.(Negative)

(c) It reflects the whole world like a mirror. (Interrogative)

(d) We can not help reading newspaper daily. (Affirmative)

(e) It contains daily news. (Passive)

(f) We are helped in many ways by it. (Active)

(g) By reading newspaper, we can enrich our knowledge. (Negative)

(h) It is called the people's parliament. (Active)

(i) Nothing is so important as it. ( Comparative)

(j) We should read newspaper to know the outside world more. (Imperative)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) The newspaper is unquestionably one of the most valuable sources of knowledge.

(b) Unfortunately, it lacks both local and international news.

(c) Does it mirror the entire world like a reflection?

(d) Reading the newspaper daily is unavoidable. Daily news is contained within.

(f) It actively aids us in numerous ways.

(g) Enriching our knowledge can be achieved by reading the newspaper.

(h) People fondly refer to it as the people's parliament.

(i) There is nothing more important than it.

(j) We should read the newspaper to gain a better understanding of the outside world.

Explanation:
(a) Newspaper is a useful source of knowledge.
Explanation: Changed the superlative “one of the most useful” to the positive degree by using “a useful” to state a general quality.

(b) It does not carry only local news; it also carries international news.
Explanation: Made the sentence negative by adding “does not” and clarified the contrast with “also” to keep the original meaning.

(c) Does it reflect the whole world like a mirror?
Explanation: Turned the statement into a yes/no question by using the auxiliary “does” and inverting subject and verb.

(d) We read the newspaper daily.
Explanation: Removed the negative structure “cannot help” and used a simple affirmative present tense to express the habitual action.

(e) Daily news is contained in it.
Explanation: Formed the passive by making the object “daily news” the subject and using the passive verb “is contained.”

(f) It helps us in many ways.
Explanation: Converted the passive “are helped in many ways by it” to active with “it” as subject and “helps” as the verb.

(g) We cannot enrich our knowledge by reading the newspaper.
Explanation: Made the sentence negative by changing “can” to “cannot,” which negates the possibility expressed originally.

(h) People call it the people's parliament.
Explanation: Changed the passive “is called” to an active form with the agent “People” and the verb “call.”

(i) It is more important than anything.
Explanation: Converted the original “Nothing is so important as it” into a comparative form using “more... than.”

(j) Read the newspaper to know the outside world better.
Explanation: Turned the sentence into an imperative by using the base verb “Read,” implying the subject “you,” and used “better” for clearer comparative meaning.

Question #4 (ID: 481766)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the gaps with suitable prepositions, articles and zero articles (a, an, the or x):

Rangamati is one of (a)..............most attractive hilly districts of Bangladesh. It is located (b)...............the western bank of Kaptai lake. Most of the visitors visit the place for its (c)................eye-catching natural beauty. Nature has adorned this town (d)................all the elements of beauty. (e)..................hills covered with green trees present (f)..............unique sight. There are many tourist spots here. The suspension bridge of Rangamati is (g)................ attraction for the tourists. It is also a home of several (h).................. ethnic groups (i)...............trip to Rangamati would be (j)................ outstanding experience for the nature lovers.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) the; (b) in; (c) x; (d) with; (e) The; (f) a; (g) an; (h) x; (i) A; (j) an.

Explanation:
Answers: (a) the; (b) on the; (c) x; (d) with; (e) the; (f) a; (g) an; (h) x; (i) a; (j) an.

Explanation: Use a "the" in (a) because "one of the most" requires the definite article with a superlative, and in (e) because specific hills of the town are meant. Use "on the" in (b) for location with "western bank," and "with" in (d) to show accompaniment. Use "a"/"an" for single countable nouns ((f), (i), (g), (j)) choosing "an" before a vowel sound; omit the article (x) after a possessive ("its" in (c)) and after a quantifier ("several" in (h)).

Question #5 (ID: 481767)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the blanks with suitable prepositions or articles. Put cross (x) for zero article.

Computers are used (a)__________ many ways. For example, (b)_________ computer's memory may carry the names, addresses and flight numbers of air plane passengers. (c)_________ ticket agent can find (d)_________ almost instantly, by typing (e)___________ flight number, whether there is a seat available (f)_________ a particular plane. At flight time, the computer can make a list of all the passengers (g)________ the plane. Computers can also solve many problems. (h)___________ many bits of information can be compared (i)___________ one another. Mathematical calculations can then be performed (j)__________ them.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

(a) in; (b) a; (c) A; (d) out; (e) a; (f) on/in; (g) of; (h) x; (i) with; (j) with.

Explanation:
Answers: (a) in, (b) a, (c) A, (d) out, (e) the, (f) on, (g) on, (h) x, (i) with, (j) on.

Explanation: Use [math]"in"[/math] for manner ("in many ways"); use the indefinite article [math]"a"[/math] for a non-specific computer and [math]"A"[/math] at the start of a sentence; [math]"find out"[/math] is a phrasal verb so [math]"out"[/math] is needed; [math]"the flight number"[/math] is specific; [math]"on"[/math] denotes location with a plane; no article (x) before plural [math]"many bits"[/math]; [math]"with"[/math] is used for comparison and [math]"on"[/math] for performing operations on data.

Question #6 (ID: 481768)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the blanks with suitable prepositions or articles. Some of the blanks may not require a preposition or an article. Put across (x) in those blanks:

There is no doubt that youth is (a)________best time of (b)________life. This is the time when it is (c)_________ most important (d)_________ one to remember (e)_______ maxim, "As you sow, so shall you reap." One must sow (f) __________ seeds (g)__________ industry, truthfulness and other virtues (h)________ this season (i)_________ reap the harvest of prosperity and happiness. Whatever takes root in a man (j)_________ this time lasts throughout the rest of his life and moulds his future.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

(a) the; (b) x; (c) x; (d) for; (e) the; (f) the; (g) of; (h) in; (i) to; (j) at.

Explanation:
Answers: (a) the, (b) one's, (c) — (no word), (d) for, (e) the, (f) the, (g) of, (h) in, (i) to, (j) at.

Explanation: Use "the" for specific nouns ("the best time", "the maxim", "the seeds") and "one's" to show possession of "life"; no article is needed before "most important" because it's a predicate adjective. "For" introduces the logical subject ("for one to remember"), "of" shows what the seeds consist of, "in this season" gives the time/place of sowing, "to reap" indicates purpose, and "at this time" denotes when something takes root.

Question #7 (ID: 481769)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the gaps with suitable prepositions, articles and zero articles (a, an, the or x):

George Washington was the first president of America This great man was obedient (a)___________ his parents.(b)_________ the age of 15 he decided to go (c)____________ studies at (d)____________ excellent school in Europe, where his brother was studying and had made all (e)_____________ preparations for crossing (f)____________ Atlantic Ocean. He ordered his people to put his necessary things (g)__________ the ship. As he was preparing to leave, he went to see his (h)__________ mother. She was not happy thinking that her son had to struggle (i) __________ lot to acquire (j)_________education only at 15. So, Washington did not go.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

(a) to; (b) At; (c) for; (d) an; (e) the; (f) the; (g) in; (h) x; (i) a; (j) x;

Explanation:
Answers: (a) to, (b) at, (c) for, (d) an, (e) the, (f) the, (g) on, (h) his, (i) a, (j) an.

Explanation: Use the fixed prepositional collocations—“obedient to,” “at the age,” “go for studies,” “put … on the ship,” “crossing the Atlantic,” “struggle a lot,” and the possessive “his mother.” Article rules: use [math]an[/math] before a vowel sound (“an excellent,” “an education”), use [math]the[/math] for a definite/specified noun already identified (“the preparations,” “the Atlantic”), and use [math]a[/math] for a nonspecific quantity (“a lot”).

Question #8 (ID: 481770)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the gaps with suitable prepositions, articles and zero articles (a, an, the orx):

Covid-19 is (a)________ infectious diseases which has taken away many lives (b)________ the world. It has created economic crisis (c)_________ many countries of the world. Many people have lost their jobs. Many small traders. compelled to leave their trades. No doubt, it is a great disaster (d)___________ the people of the world. Though the corona virus is very (e)___________ deadly, it has created awareness (f)____________ mass people. Besides we have learnt many things (g)___________ it so far. Earlier, we were indifferent (h)___________ some rules of health and hygiene. Due to Covid-19, people of the world have become more conscious regarding the rules of health. Now a days, we try to maintain social distancing. We avoid. (i)____________ massive gatherings of people. We also have made a good habit (j)___________ washing hands several times a day.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

'(a) an; (b) from; (c) in; (d) for; (e) x; (f) among; (g) for; (h) to; (i) x; (j) of.

Explanation:
(a) "an" — because we need the singular form "an infectious disease" and "infectious" begins with a vowel sound.  
(b) "around" — "around the world" is the common preposition meaning everywhere in the world.  
(c) "in" — "in many countries" shows where the economic crisis exists.  
(d) "for" — "a great disaster for the people" indicates who is affected.  
(e) "x" (no article) — no article is used before the adjective "deadly" in the predicate "is very deadly."  
(f) "among" — "awareness among mass people" (better: "among the masses") shows awareness within a group.  
(g) "from" — "learnt many things from it" shows the source of learning.  
(h) "to" — "indifferent to some rules" is the correct idiom.  
(i) "x" (no article) — no article is needed when talking generally about "massive gatherings" in plural.  
(j) "of" — the phrase is "a habit of washing hands," so "of" links habit and action.

Question #9 (ID: 481771)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the blanks with prepositions or articles. Put cross where there is needed no articles:

There are two types (a)_________ dreams. One is just (b)__________ dream and completely baseless. Anybody may meet (c)__________ it while sleeping. Another dream is real. It is very desirable to (d)__________ conscious and great person. Generally, it is called (e)__________future plan. To be a great person this dream is (f)___________must. Then go ahead (g)__________ the working field. Really, if there is no real dream, there is no interest (h)__________action. True successfully depends (i)____________ a real dream. Remember, a life without (j)____________ aim or dream is like a ship without a rudder.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

(a) of; (b) a; (c) with; (d) the; (e) a; (f) a; (g) with; (h) in; (i) on; (j) an.

Explanation:
Answers: (a) of, (b) a, (c) — (no word), (d) be a, (e) a, (f) a, (g) in, (h) in, (i) on, (j) an.

Use 'of' after "types"; use 'a' or 'an' with singular countable nouns (e.g., "a dream," "a future plan," "a must," "an aim"); (c) needs no article or preposition because "meet it" is complete. Use 'in' for being within a field or showing interest ("in the working field," "interest in action"), and 'on' for dependence ("depends on a real dream"); 'to be a' is the correct infinitive phrase in (d).

Question #10 (ID: 481772)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the blanks with suitable prepositions or articles. Some of the blanks may not require a preposition or an article. Put a cross (x) in those blanks:

There is no doubt that youth is (a)_________best time of (b)___________life. This is the time when it is (c)_________most important (d)_________ one to remember (e)_________ maxim. "As you sow, so shall you reap." One must sow (f)___________ seeds (g)__________ industry, truthfulness and other virtues (h)__________ this season (i)__________ reap the harvest of prosperity and happiness. Whatever takes root in a man (j)__________ this time lasts throughout the rest of his life and moulds his future.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

(a) the; (b) x; (c) x; (d) for; (e) the; (f) the; (g) of; (h) in; (i) to; (j).at.

Explanation:
Explanation: a "the" is required because "best" is a superlative and takes the definite article; b is a cross (x) because "life" is used in a general sense and needs no article.  
c is x (no word) because "most important" works as the predicate adjective; d "for" introduces who should act ("one"); e "the" specifies that particular maxim.  
f "the" and g "of" form the phrase "the seeds of …"; h "in" indicates the season (time) when they are sown and i "to" shows purpose ("to reap"); j "during" correctly denotes the period when something takes root.

Question #11 (ID: 481709)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Bangladesh is a (a) — (river) and (b) — (agriculture) country. So, we cannot ignore the (c) — (important) of rivers. Our agriculture is largely (d) — (depend) on the rivers. But we get (e) — (sufficient) water for use from the rivers. There are (f) — (differ) reasons behind it. At first the water of many rivers (g) — (dry) up in summer. Again, the water of some rivers is (h) — (extreme) poisonous. This poisonous water is (i) — (suit) for our agriculture. So, water pollution should be prevented at any cost for the (j) — (better) of our agriculture.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
(a) and (b): use adjectives to describe the country, so "riverine" and "agricultural" are correct.  
(c): a noun is needed, so "importance." (d): an adjective, "dependent." (e): the sentence means lack of enough water, so "insufficient."  
(f): adjective "different." (g): present tense verb for rivers, "dries." (h): adverb modifying "poisonous," so "extremely." (i): negative adjective "unsuitable." (j): noun "betterment."

Question #12 (ID: 481710)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Life without leisure and (a) — (relax) is dull. Nobody can work without rest. Life becomes (b) — (charm) if one doesn’t have any time to enjoy (c) — (beauty) objects of nature. Work becomes (d) — (monotony) if there is no break in it! It hinders the (e) — (smooth) of life. Leisure (f) — (new) our spirit to work. Everybody knows that (g) — (work) is (h) — (harm). Leisure doesn’t mean (i) — (idle). It gives (j) — (fresh) to our mind.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Life needs the correct word forms to fit grammar and meaning: the answers are (a) relaxation, (b) charmless, (c) beautiful, (d) monotonous, (e) smoothness, (f) renews, (g) overwork, (h) harmful, (i) idleness, (j) freshness. Each choice matches the required part of speech in context (nouns like "relaxation/smoothness/idleness/freshness", adjectives like "charmless/beautiful/monotonous/harmful", the verb "renews", and the compound noun "overwork"). These are standard derivations (suffixes like -less, -ous, -ness, -ful, and the verb form -s) that make the sentence grammatically correct and meaningful.

Question #13 (ID: 481711)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Those who lead a (a) — (luxury) life, are always (b) — (different) to the miseries of the poor. They enjoy life in (c) — (amuse) and (d) — (merry). They are (e) — (centered) people. They have little (f) — (realize) of the (g) — (bounded) sufferings of the poor. They remain indifferent to their (h) — (suffer). They feel (i) — (comfort) to work for their (j) — (better).

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Each blank takes the correct derived form: "luxurious" (adj from luxury), "indifferent" (negative adjective), "amusement" and "merriment" (nouns for enjoyment), "self-centered" (adj), "realization" (noun), "boundless" (opposite of bounded), "sufferings" (noun), "comfortable" (adj) and "betterment" (noun). Use adjective forms when describing people or attitudes and noun forms when naming states or things, and apply common prefixes/suffixes (in-, -ous, -ion, -ment, -less) to make the meanings fit the sentence.

Question #14 (ID: 481712)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In ancient time, textbook was the most (a) — (resource) thing for the students. Teachers were the only guides and source of information. The students had to collect all the (b) — (inform) from the lecture of their (c) — (teach). There was no guidebook or other (d) — (refer) books in the market. During that period a teacher had to deliver a lecture by (e) — (study) the textbook. Because of the (f) — (situate) the students used to depend on the teachers (g) — (complete). As a result, there was a great (h) — (relate) between a (i) — (teach) and a student. Their (j) — (popular) existed among the students in the society.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
(a) "resourceful" — we need an adjective from "resource" to describe the textbook as rich in resources/information.  
(b) "information" — the noun form of "inform" fits "collect all the ___."  
(c) "teacher" — the noun form of "teach" names the person giving the lecture.  
(d) "reference" — used before "books," the noun/adjective "reference" denotes books for consultation.  
(e) "studying" — the gerund form fits after "by" to show how the teacher prepared the lecture.  
(f) "situation" — the noun form of "situate" refers to the context or condition causing dependence.  
(g) "completely" — the adverb form of "complete" modifies "depend" to show extent.  
(h) "relationship" — a noun from "relate" that expresses the connection between teacher and student.  
(i) "teacher" — again the correct noun form of "teach" for the person.  
(j) "popularity" — the noun form of "popular" shows how well liked they were among students.

So, they got a (j) — (respect) position in the society.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:

Again, he can start his day’s work (e) — (early) than others. An early riser does not suffer from (f) — (physic) problems very often. So, he need not go to any (g) — (physic) (h) — (frequent). Thus, an early riser enjoys (i) — (vary) benefits and leads a (j) — (peace) life.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) getting; (b) riser; (c) freshness; (d) melodious; (e) earlier; (f) physical; (g) physician; (h) frequently; (i) various; (j) peaceful.

Explanation:

Question:
Zahir Raihan was one of the most (a) — (talent) filmmakers in Bangladesh. He was an (b) — (act) worker of the Language Movement. He was also present at the (c) — (history) meeting at Amtala on February 21, 1952. All through his life, Zahir dreamt for a (d) — (democrat) society, a society that will (e) — (sure) freedom of speech and will. He made a — (legend) film Jibon Theke Neya based on the Language (g) — (Move) of 1952. He could see the (h) — (incept) of a free and (i) — (dependent) Bangladesh. And it’s a pity that this (j) — (dream) was missing at such a time when his dream came true.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) talented; (b) active; (c) historical; (d) democratic; (e) ensure; (f) legendary; (g) Movement; (h) inception; (i) independent; (j) dreamer.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ক talented — 'most' এর সঙ্গে যোগ্য বিশেষণ হলে 'talented' সঠিক; খ active — আন্দোলনের কর্মী হলে 'active worker' ব্যবহার হয়; গ historic — গুরুত্বপূর্ণ ঘটনার জন্য 'historic' (historical হল ইতিহাসসংবলিত) উপযুক্ত; ঘ democratic — 'democratic society' ঠিকভাবে সমাজবাদের বর্ননা করে; ঙ ensure — স্বাধীনতা নিশ্চিত করা মানে 'ensure' (ক্রিয়া) লাগে; চ legendary — প্রসিদ্ধ চলচ্চিত্র বোঝাতে 'legendary' ব্যবহৃত হয়; ছ Movement — 'Language Movement' (আন্দোলনের নাম) সঠিক; জ inception — কোনো স্বাধীন রাষ্ট্রের উদ্বোধন/শুরু বোঝাতে 'inception' উপযুক্ত; ঝ independent — 'free and independent Bangladesh' বলতে 'independent' লাগে; ঞ dream — এখানে সাধারণ নাউনেরূপ 'dream' পরিবর্তন ছাড়া ঠিক।  সংক্ষেপে, প্রতিটি খালি স্থানে শব্দের ব্যাকরণিক রূপ (বিশেষণ/ক্রিয়া/নাম) অনুযায়ী উপযুক্ত রূপ বসানো হয়েছে।

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) education; (b) useful; (c) truly; (d) personal; (e) thoughtful; (f) truthful; (g) dutiful; (h) prosperous; (i) remove; (j) self-reliance.

Explanation:
Choose the form that fits the grammar: noun where a thing is needed, adjective/adverb where something is described, and verb where an action is meant. For example, (a) "education" is a noun (the aim of something), (b) "useful" is an adjective after "be", (c) "truly" is an adverb modifying "educated", (d) "personal", (e) "thoughtful", (f) "truthful", (g) "dutiful" and (h) "prosperous" are adjectives describing nouns, (i) "remove" is the verb meaning "take away", and (j) "self-reliance" is a noun. Changing roots with the right prefixes/suffixes makes them the correct parts of speech and keeps the sentence grammatically correct.

It is a good (g) — (company) in our solitary hours. It helps the (h) — (grow) of public opinion. But it is not an (i) — (mix) blessing. However, newspaper has made the world (j) — (small) and help one nation to understand the other.

Options:

Explanation:
Explanation:

Solution:
(a) dishonesty; (b) harmful; (c) injustice; (d) immoral; (e) uncomfortable; (f) responsible; (g) honesty; (h) dishonesty; (i) loved; (f) prosperity.

Question #39 (ID: 481737)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Money cannot buy (a) ----- (happy). Money is (b) ------ (obvious) necessary for our life. But is not the thing that (c) ------ (necessary)----- brings happiness. Happiness is (d)------ a psychological thing. Basically, it is the name of a (e)------ (feel)------. It lies in the (f)-------- (content) of mind. A poor man with mental (g)------- (satisfy)----- may become really happy in life. On the other hand, a man with a lot of (h) ------ (rich)------ may not be happy. Their wealth becomes the cause of (i) ------ (happy) because most of the time they suffer from (j) ----- (suffer) So they lead a life full of cares and anxieties.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) happiness: (b) obviously; (c) necessarily; (d) absolutely; (e) feeling; (f) contentment; (g) satisfaction; (h) riches; (i) unhappiness; (j) insecurity.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক এখানে ক্রিয়াপদ "buy"‑এর উদ্দেশ্যে নাম (object) লাগবে; "happy" বিশেষণ, তাই নামবাচক রূপ "happiness" ব্যবহৃত হবে।  
খ "necessary" একটি বিশেষণ, এটিকে বর্ণনা করার জন্য ক্রিয়া বা বিশেষণের ওপর কাজ করে এমন ক্রিয়াবিশেষণ (adverb) লাগবে — তাই "obviously" সঠিক।  
গ "brings"‑কে বা পুরো ভাবকে নির্দেশ করার জন্য adverb প্রয়োজন; "necessarily" এই কাজে উপযুক্ত।  
ঘ এখানে বলা হচ্ছে সুখ মূলত মানসিক বিষয়, তাই তা বর্ণনা করতে "primarily" (অর্থাৎ প্রধানত/মূলত) ব্যবহার করা হয়।  
ঙ "the name of a ..." পর নেওয়ার জন্য名詞 প্রয়োজন; অনুভূতির অর্থে "feeling" সঠিক নামবাচক শব্দ।  
চ "content of mind" বলতে মনের সন্তুষ্টি বোঝাতে নামবাচক রূপ "contentment" প্রয়োজন।  
ছ "mental ..." বলতে মানসিক সন্তুষ্টির কথা, তাই ক্রিয়ার পরিবর্তে নাম "satisfaction" সঠিক।  
জ "a lot of ..." এর পরে বস্তুবাচক শবদ চাই; "rich" বিশেষণ, তাই বস্তুবাচক "riches" অর্থাৎ ধন-সম্পদ ব্যবহার হবে।  
ঝ "the cause of ..." পর সাধারণত নাম লাগে এবং "happy"‑এর বিপরীত বোঝাতে "unhappiness" যথাযথ।  
ঞ "suffer from" এর পরে ক্রিয়া নয় বরং নাম/ক্রিয়ানাম (gerund) লাগে; ফলে "suffering" ব্যবহার করা হয়।

Question #40 (ID: 481738)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\begin{array}{|l|l|} \hline \text{stand} & \text{become} & \text{see} & \text{go}& \text{cause}& \text{remain}& \text{ply}& \text{know}& \text{take}\\ \hline \end{array}[/math]

On a rainy day it (a)----- all day long. The sky is overcast with thick clouds. The sky is not (b)------ None can (c) ------out without an umbrella. Water (d) -------on roads. As a result, roads (e)------ muddy and slippery. In Dhaka city, the roads and streets (f) ------- under water for hours together (g)------ much inconvenience to the pedestrians. On some roads motorized vehicles or even rickshaws can (h)--------. The sufferings of the city dwellers (i)------ already (j) some steps to solve this problem.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) freedom; (b) warrior; (c) independence; (d) dearer; (e) willingly; (f) mighty; (g) mainly; (h) fighter; (i) unknown; (j) disappeared.

Explanation:

Question #43 (ID: 481741)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the text adding suffixes, prefixes or the both to the root words given in the parentheses:

Facebook is a social (a)................. (network) site. It has gained much (b).............(popular) among the young (c)................generate. Sometimes, our young generation waste their (d)..............(value) time by (e)...............(browse) facebook. So, in this respect parental (f)...............(supervise) is a must. Many people (g)...................(fine) facebook as an (h)................(embarrass) (i).................(invade) on others' (j)...................(person) privacy. However, it plays a (k)................. (signify) role in (l)................(socialize) as well as (m)...................(nature) understanding and (n).............. (operation).

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) networking; (b) popularity; (c) generation; (d) valuable; (e) browsing; (f) supervision; (g) define; (h) embarrassing; (i) invasion; (j) personal; (k) significant; (1) socialization; (m) natural; (n) cooperation.

Explanation:
Facebook is a social networking (network) site. It has gained much popularity (popular) among the young generation (generate). Sometimes, our young generation waste their valuable (value) time by browsing (browse) Facebook. So, in this respect parental supervision (supervise) is a must. Many people define (fine) Facebook as an embarrassing (embarrass) invasion (invade) of others' personal (person) privacy. However, it plays a significant (signify) role in socialization (socialize) as well as natural (nature) understanding and cooperation (operation).

Explanation:
I changed word forms by adding appropriate prefixes/suffixes so each word fits the sentence grammatically (e.g., verbs to nouns: "popularity", "invasion"; verb to gerund: "browsing"; noun to adjective: "personal", "natural"). Prefixes like "de-" and "co-" create correct meanings ("define", "cooperation"), and adjectival endings like "-ing" or "-able" make words modify nouns properly ("networking", "valuable").

Question:
Complete the text adding prefixes, suffixes or both to the root words given in the parenthesis:

Bangladesh is mainly a (a)______(river)_______and (b)______(agriculture)______country. (c)_______(major)______of her people live in villages and most of them are farmers. (d)_______(fortunate), the condition of our farmers is (e)______(satisfactory______They can (f)_______(hard)______lead a _______ carefree life. Their life is full of miseries and (g)_______ (advantages) _______ They can't plough their land (h)______(proper)______due to (i)______ (finance)______ and (j)______ (technology) _______ support. They need assistance from the (k)______ (govern)______ to come out of their age-old (1)______ (convention)_______ method. Scientific system of cultivation is going to be (m) ______ (gradual)_______ successful and (n)_______(effect)_______.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) riverine; (b) agricultural; (c) Majority; (d) Unfortunately; (e) unsatisfactory; (f) hardly; (g) disadvantages; (h) properly; (i) financial; (j) technological; (k) government; (1) conventional; (m) gradually; (n) effective.

Explanation:
Explanation: Use the correct word-forms (adjective, noun or adverb) made by adding suitable prefixes/suffixes to fit the grammar and meaning. For example, "riverine" and "agricultural" are adjectives describing the country, and "majority" is the noun meaning most people. Negative ideas use the prefix "un-" or "dis-" as in "unfortunately," "unsatisfactory," and "disadvantages"; adverbs take "-ly" (e.g., "hardly," "properly," "gradually"). Other common suffixes produce adjectives or nouns: "financial," "technological," "government" (from govern + -ment), "conventional," and "effective," which all match the roles required in the sentences.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete. the text adding suffixes, prefixes or both with the root words given in the parenthesis:

In ancient time, textbook was the most (a)________ (resource)_________ thing for a student. (b)_________ (teach)__________were only guides and source of (c)__________ (inform)_________ The students had to collect all (d)_________(inform)___________ news from their teachers. There was hardly any guide book or other (e)___________ (refer)_________ book in the market. So, teachers gave (f)__________ (delive)_________ of a lecture by studying the text books, and so the students had (g)__________ (depend)_________on their teachers (h)________ (proficient)__________ As a result, there existed (i)___________ (measure)__________ relationship between them. The (j)__________ (popular)__________ of these great teachers was never on the wane. Students had (k)_________ (devote)__________ to maintain a healthy relation with their (l)___________ (honour)___________ teachers. Teachers also maintained an ever bond of (m)___________ (friend)__________with their (n)__________ (affection)__________ students.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) resourceful; (b) Teachers; (c) information; (d) informative; (e) reference; (f) delivery; (g) dependence; (h) proficiency; (i) immeasurable; (j) popularity; (k) devotion; (1) honourable; (m) friendship; (n) affectionate.

Explanation:
Explanation: The blanks are filled by changing the root words into the grammatical form required by the sentence using common suffixes and prefixes: use [-er] to form agent nouns (teach → teachers), [-ion]/[-ation] to make abstract nouns (inform → information; devote → devotion), [-ful]/[-ive] to make adjectives (resource → resourceful; inform → informative), and [-ship], [-ity], [-ence]/[-ance] to make friendship, popularity, dependence respectively. Use the negative prefix im- with an adjective-forming suffix to negate a root when needed (measure → immeasurable). Choosing these forms makes the sentence grammatically correct because each blank requires either a noun, adjective, or agent noun that matches the surrounding words.

The purpose of (a)__________(educate) is to make a man fully (b)_________(equip) to be (c)_________(use) to himself and to society. A (d)_________ (true) educated person should be self-reliant with regard to his (e)___________ (person) needs. He should be well-mannered (f)__________ (thought), sympathetic and (g)__________(operative) He should be (h)_________ (truth), honest, punctual and (i)__________ (duty). (j)_________ (punctual) is a virtue that_________ makes a nation (k)__________ (prosper). An. educated person tries to (l)___________ (move) the (m)_________ (suffer) of his countrymen. He also helps others in attaining (n)__________ (self-reliant).

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) education; (b) equipped; (c) useful; (d) truly; (e) personal; (f) thoughtful; (g) cooperative; (h) truthful: (i) dutiful; (j) Punctuality;. (k) prosperous; (1) remove; (m) sufferings; (n) self-reliance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Question:
Complete the text adding suffixes, prefixes or the both to the root words given in the parenthesis:

Vocabulary is very important in learning a language properly. To (a)__________(rich) your vocabulary, you have to read books and learn new words by knowing their meanings (b)__________(accurate). You may use a dictionary to know the (c)_________ (known) words or try to understand the (d)___________ (context) meaning of them. Repeated reading will help you understand the (e)_________ use them in (g)_________ (i)_______ (specify) topic (f)_________ (clear) and (vary) situations. Language learning is a (h)___________ (continue) process and your (i)_________(proficient) will come today or tomorrow. What is needed most is (j)___________ (continue). It also needs your (k)__________ from (m)__________ (sincere). A common language is required for (l)___________ (interact) among people from (m)_______(differ) countries and contexts. Without a common language it is difficult to perform activities at the (n)______(nation) level. English has assumed the position of that common language.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) enrich; (b) accurately; (c) unknown; (d) contextual; (e) specific; (f) clearly; (g) various; (h) continuous (i) proficiency; (j) continuity; (k) sincerity; (1) interaction; (m) different; (n) international.

Explanation:
The blanks are filled by adding common prefixes/suffixes: en- + rich = enrich; accurate + -ly = accurately; un- + known = unknown; context + -ual = contextual; specify + -ic = specific; vary + -ed = varied; clear can remain “clear” in “clear situations.” Other forms: continue + -ous = continuous; proficient → proficiency; continue → continuity; sincere → sincerity; interact → interaction; differ → different; nation → national. These follow basic word‑formation rules: prefixes (en-, un-) change meaning, and suffixes (-ly, -al, -ic, -ed, -ous, -ency/-ity/-ion) change word class so each word fits grammatically and semantically in the sentence.

Question #48 (ID: 481746)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the text adding suffixes, prefixes or the both with the root words given in the parenthesis:

Bangladesh is blessed with many seasons. Winter is one of them. It is the (a)_________(cold)________of all seasons. It is usually (b)_______(rain)_________ Though ours is a small country, the (c) _________ (cold)________of Winter is not (d)________ (equal) felt in all regions. In some regions, (e)_________ (special)_________ in the (f)________ (north)________districts, people experience (g)___________(bite)__________ cold in winter. Nature looks dull and (h)___________ (gloom). During night and morning, the whole of nature remains (i)__________ (cover)___________ with fog and mist. Then the poor suffer (j)___________ (great)__________ for want of warm___________ clothes. Again in some (k)_____________ (hill) areas there is (l)____________(severe)___________ of cold. (m)____________ (where) in the vast (n)____________ (south) areas people experience less cold.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) coldest; (b) rainless; (c) coldness; (d) equally; (e) specially; (f) northern; (g) bitter; (h) gloomy; (i) covered; (j) greatly; (k) hilly; (1) severity; (m) Whereas; (n) southern; 8. Tag Questions,

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক "coldest" — 'cold' থেকে সর্বোচ্চ বিভিন্নতা (superlative) করতে '-est' যোগ করে 'coldest' হয়, কারণ বাক্যে তুলনা করা হচ্ছে।  
খ "rainless" — 'rain' + '-less' মানে 'বৃষ্টি নেই/অপচিকিত', তাই শীত সাধারণত বৃষ্টিহীন বলতে 'rainless' ব্যবহৃত হয়।  
গ "coldness" — 'cold' থেকে abstract noun বানাতে '-ness' যোগ করে 'coldness' হয়, যা শীতের তীব্রতা বোঝায়।  
ঘ "equally" — 'equal' এর adverb হলো 'equally', কারণ 'felt' ক্রিয়াটিকে কিভাবে অনুভূত হয়েছে তা বর্ণনা করতে adverb লাগে।  
ঙ "especially" — 'special' থেকে adverb 'especially' হয়, যা নির্দিষ্টভাবে কোথায় তা নির্দেশ করে।  
চ "northern" — দিকবাচক adjective 'north' → 'northern' ব্যবহার করে উত্তর জেলা বোঝানো হয়।  
ছ "biting" — 'bite' থেকে present participle/ adjective 'biting' দিয়ে 'biting cold' নামক idiom অনুযায়ী তীক্ষ্ণ শীত বোঝায়।  
জ "gloomy" — 'gloom' থেকে adjective করতে '-y' যোগ করে 'gloomy' হয়, যা প্রকৃতির বিষণ্ণ অবস্থা দেখায়।  
ঝ "covered" — 'cover' এর past participle 'covered' ব্যবহার করে অবস্থা (remains covered with fog) বোঝানো হয়।  
ট "greatly" — 'great' থেকে adverb 'greatly' হয়ে 'suffer' ক্রিয়াকে পরিমাপ করে (ভেবে বড় কষ্ট ভোগ করা)।  
(উক্ত বাক্যে) "warm woollen clothes" — শীত প্রতিরোধে 'woollen' ধাতু-শব্দ যোগ করে উষ্ণ কাপড় নির্দেশ করা হয়।  
ঠ "hilly" — 'hill' থেকে adjective 'hilly' করে পাহাড়ি অঞ্চলের বর্ণনা করা হয়।  
ড "severity" — 'severe' থেকে abstract noun 'severity' হয়, যা শীতের তীব্রতার মাত্রা প্রকাশ করে।  
ঢ "whereas" — 'where' থেকে 'whereas' একটি বিরোধসূচক conjunction, বিপরীত অবস্থা দেখাতে লাগে।  
ণ "southern" — 'south' → 'southern' করে দক্ষিণাঞ্চল adjectivally চিহ্নিত করা হয়।

Question #49 (ID: 481747)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the text adding suffixes, prefixes or the both with the root words given in the parenthesis:

Mr. Peter is a good student. He is very (a)___________ (study). He is always (b)____________ (mind) to his studies and also (c)___________ (duty) to his daily activities. He is very (d)___________ (respect), to his elders. He is (c)____________ (truth) also. Weak students find him as a (f)____________ (help) figure. His (g)___________ (think) power is admirable. He is really (h)__________ (create) in any writing. He never forgets the benefit of (i)______________ (punctual). (j)___________ (sincere) is another quality of his daily activities. He is also an early (k)____________ (rise). Any problem cannot make him (l)____________ (attentive). He always behaves very (m)____________ (polite) with every person. His (n)____________ (honest) cannot be expressed in a word.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) studious; (b) mindful; (c) dutiful; (d) respectful; (e) truthful; (f) helpful; (g) thinking; (h) creative; (i) punctuality; (j) Sincerity; (k) riser; (1) inattentive; (m) politely; (n) honesty.

Explanation:
Most blanks are filled by adding suffixes or prefixes to make the root word the correct part of speech: adjectives use endings like -ous/-ious (study → studious) or -ful (mindful, helpful, dutiful, respectful, truthful), -ive (creative); adverbs use -ly (polite → politely); nouns use -ity/-ness (punctual → punctuality, sincere → sincerity, honest → honesty); the negative prefix in- makes inattentive; and -ing or -er give verbal/adjectival forms (thinking, riser). Choose the form that fits the sentence grammar (adjective before a noun, adverb after “behaves,” noun after “benefit of,” negative with in- when expressing “not”).

Question #50 (ID: 481748)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the text adding suffixes, prefixes or the both with the root words given in the parenthesis:

The freedom fighters are the (a)____________ (hero) sons of our land. They fought to save our (b)____________(gold) Bangla in 1971. We have got the (c)___________ (independent) of our loving motherland by their (d)______________ (super) sacrifice. Some of the (e)______________ (free) fighters are still (f)_____________ (live). Most of the freedom (g)_____________ (fight) are now (h)_____________ (actual) above 70 years old. (i)____________ (deed), we are very (j)_____________ (luck) to see them (k)______________ (direct). As they are our heroic sons, we should respect them (l)____________ (profound). We must remember them (m)____________ (ever). Because they laid down their lives (n)_____________ (keep) all behind.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Adding suffix, prefix or both:

(a) heroic; (b) golden; (c) independence; (d) supreme; (e) freedom; (f) alive; (g) fighters; (h) actually; (i) Indeed; (j) lucky; (k) directly; (1) profoundly; (m) forever; (n) keeping.

Explanation:
a "heroic" — the adjective form of "hero" used to describe the sons (people) who show heroism.  
b "golden" — adjective from "gold" used figuratively to praise Bangla (e.g., "golden Bangla").  
c "independence" — the noun form of "independent" meaning the state we obtained.  
d "supreme" — from "super"; "supreme sacrifice" is the correct collocation meaning the highest sacrifice.  
e "freedom" — noun formed from "free"; "freedom fighters" is the standard compound.  
f "alive" — adjective meaning still living; "still alive" correctly describes people who live.  
g "fighters" — plural noun from "fight" to match "freedom fighters."  
h "actually" — adverb from "actual" used to state the fact ("are actually above 70").  
i "Indeed" — sentence adverb for emphasis, fitting at the start of the sentence.  
j "lucky" — adjective from "luck" describing our good fortune.  
k "directly" — adverb from "direct" modifying "see" to mean "in person."  
l "profoundly" — adverb from "profound" meaning deeply; "respect them profoundly" is correct.  
m "forever" — adverb from "ever" meaning for all time, as in "remember them forever."  
n "to keep" — the infinitive shows purpose: they "laid down their lives to keep..."

Moreover, there are (e)---- (honest) people who cut trees for making money (f)----- (legally). The (g)---- (remove) of trees causes serious damage to the soil as trees give (h)---- (protect) to soil as well. The temperature will rise and it will cause green house effect. One day the country will be (i)---- (suitable) for living. So, tree (j)----- (plant) programme should be extended throughout the country.

Options:

Question #54 (ID: 481752)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Everybody knows that (a)---- (smoke) is a (b)---- (danger) bad habit. It is (c)---- (harm) to health. It is also (d)---- (cost). A (e)---- (smoke) should not smoke (f)---- (public). Smoking creates (g)---- (pollute). A single puff of cigarette contains. (h)---- (numerable) harmful particles that cause many (i)---- (respirator) diseases which are incurable. But there are many people who are (j)---- (aware) of the bad effects of smoking.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) smoking; (b) dangerous; (c) harmful; (d) costly; (e) smoker; (f) publicly; (g) pollution; (h) innumerable; (i) respiratory; (j) unaware.

Explanation:
Use 'smoking' (a gerund) because we need the noun for the habit; 'dangerous' (b), 'harmful' (c) and 'costly' (d) are the adjective forms that correctly describe the habit and its effects. 'Smoker' (e) names the person who smokes, 'in public' (f) is the proper prepositional phrase, 'pollution' (g) is the noun from 'pollute', and 'numerous' (h) is the correct adjective meaning many. 'Respiratory' (i) is the adjective relating to breathing, and 'unaware' (j) correctly shows people who do not know the bad effects.

Question #56 (ID: 481754)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Life without leisure and (a)---- (relax) is dull. Life becomes (b)---- (charm) if one does not have any time to enjoy the (c)---- (beauty) objects of nature. (d)----- (monotony) work hinders the (e)---- (smooth) of work. Leisure (f)---- (rich) our spirit to work. Everybody knows that (g)---- (work) is (h)---- (harm). Leisure does not mean (i)---- (idle). It gives freshness to (j)----- (create) our energy.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) relaxation; (b) charmless; (c) beautiful; (d) Monotonous; (e) smoothness; (f) enriches; (g) overwork; (h) harmful; (i) idleness; (j) recreate.

Explanation:
Leisure and relaxation are both nouns, so (a) relaxation fits; life described as lacking appeal is "charmless" and the things of nature are "beautiful," so (b) charmless and (c) beautiful. Repetition needs adjectives/nouns: (d) monotonous (adj) work hinders the (e) smoothness (noun) of work. 

(f) "Leisure enriches" uses the correct verb form; (g) overwork is the single-word noun for excessive work and (h) harmful is the adjective from harm; (i) idleness (noun) means being idle; and (j) recreate (verb) means to renew or restore our energy.

Question:
Most of the books of famous (a) — (write) are put on sale in the book fair. Most of the (b) — (visit) buy different (c) — (publish). Almost no visitor returns from the fair without making any purchase. The (d) — (buy) like to buy at a fair price. Our book fair is always (e) — (crowd). As (f) — (vary) books are (g) — (play) in a fair, the buyers get a scope to choose books. They buy (h) — (choose) books after a long search. This facility is (i) — (available) in any place other than a book fair. A book fair is always (j) — (come) to the students.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ক "writers" — কারণ এখানে 'books of famous ...' মানে বহু লেখকের বই, তাই ক্রিয়া 'write' থেকে নামবাচক বহুবচন 'writers' ব্যবহার করতে হবে।  
খ "visitors" — এখানে যারা মেলা দেখে তাদের উদ্দেশ্য, সেক্ষেত্রে 'visit' থেকে নামবাচক বহুবচন 'visitors' সঠিক।  
গ "publications" — 'publish' থেকে উৎপন্ন নামবাচক 'publication(s)' হলো বিক্রয়ের জন্য থাকা বিভিন্ন প্রকাশনা, অতএব 'publications' মানানসই।  
ঘ "buyers" — এখানে যারা কেনে তাদের বোঝাতে 'buy' থেকে নামবাচক 'buyers' (বহুবচন) ব্যবহার করা হয়।  
ঙ "crowded" — মেলার বর্ণনায় এটি একটি অবস্থা, তাই ক্রিয়ার অতীত অংশ 'crowded' অব্যয় (adjective) হিসেবে ব্যবহার করে।  
চ "various" — 'vary' থেকে গঠিত বিশেষণ 'various' ব্যবহার করলে অনেক ধরন/বিবিধ বই বোঝানো যায়।  
ছ "displayed" — এখানে বইগুলো প্রদর্শিত হওয়ার কথা বলছে, তাই passive participle 'displayed' (প্রদর্শিত) সঠিক।  
জ "chosen" — 'choose' এর অতীতভাগ 'chosen' ব্যবহার করে বোঝানো হচ্ছে দীর্ঘ অনুসন্ধানের পরে নির্বাচিত বই।  
ঝ "unavailable" — বাক্য অনুযায়ী এই সুবিধা অন্য কোথাও নেই, তাই 'available' এর নেগেটিভ রূপ 'unavailable' দরকার।  
ঞ "welcome" — 'come' থেকে গঠিত 'welcome' এখানে বিশেষণ হিসেবে ব্যবহৃত হবে: মেলা শিক্ষার্থীর কাছে সবসময় स्वागतযোগ্য/গৃহীত।

Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board

Complete the following text with right forms of verbs given in the box:


[Image]


Rivers generally (a)__________ from a mountain or a lake. They (b)__________very much important for our existence and economy. But unfortunately, we are (c)____________our rivers, choking it with toxic wastes from dyeing and textile factories. Most of the industries (d)____________waste treatment plants. These kinds of industries are (e)_____________releasing untreated liquid waste directly and (f)___________the water polluted. Our unconscious people also (g)___________different kinds of waste materials into the rivers directly. So, to keep existence of fishes and other species (h)___________in the water is impossible. Otherwise a happy, prosperous and pollution free environment for the next generation can't be (j)__________

Options:


Correct Answer:

[Image]


There are various types of fever. Dengue is one of them. It (a)_________by biting of mosquito (b)___________'Aedes'. It (c)__________ serious health hazard. Vomiting, high temperature, blood platelets etc. make the patient tormented. Many patients (d)___________if blood platelets (e)_________below 50. Living place of Aedes larva should (i)___________With a view to (j)__________ourselves aloof from mosquito bite the use of curtain is essential.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Right form of verbs:

(a) is caused; (b) named; (c) causes; (d) die; (e) go; (f) are needed; (g) get; (h) should make; (i) be destroyed; (j) keeping.

Explanation:
We use the passive "is caused" in (a) because dengue results from mosquito bites, and "called" in (b) names the mosquito; (c) takes "is a" to state a general fact. The simple present "die" (d) and "fall" (e) form a zero‑conditional showing a general cause–effect. "Are needed" (f) agrees with the plural idea "much care and proper treatment," while "in order to" requires the infinitive "keep" (g) and habitual action uses simple present "keep" (h). "Should be destroyed" (i) uses passive to show a recommended action, and "with a view to" requires the gerund "keeping" (j).

Question #72 (ID: 481688)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following text with right forms of the verbs given in the box. Use negative if necessary:


[Image]


Abdur Rahman is a student. He (a)________ in the SSC Exam this year. He (b)__________in Chattogram. He (c)__________there since his birth, but he (d)_________St. Martins Island yet. He (e)___________a lot about the beauty of St. Martin's_____________Island. (f)__________those he becomes very eager (g)__________ a visit there. As he is free now, he thinks that he___________ (h)_________the island now. (i)_________ this he becomes so excited that he (j)_____________ his friends to a meeting.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Right form of verbs:

(a) appears; (b) lives; (c) has been living; (d) did not visit; (e) hears/has heard; (f) Hearing; (g) to pay; (h) should visit; (i) Thinking; (j) calls;

Explanation:
(a) uses the present continuous "is appearing" because the exam is happening this year (an ongoing action); (b) uses simple present "lives" for a permanent fact; (c) uses present perfect "has lived" with "since his birth" to show an action continuing up to now.  
(d) is negative present perfect "has not visited" with "yet" to say the experience hasn’t happened; (e) is present perfect "has heard" for experience/information received.  
(f) is a linking phrase like "Because of this" and (g) takes the infinitive "to pay" after "eager" ("eager to pay a visit").  
(h) uses a modal like "should visit" (expressing his decision/plan) and (i)/(j) ("On this" / "calls") show the immediate result — he becomes excited and calls his friends.

Question #73 (ID: 481686)

Question:
Complete the following text with the right form of verbs given in the box :


[Image]


Most of us (a)________the wrong mentality of measuring success in life. Many poor adults (b)________ that the possession of wealth (c)________ peace of mind in life. But it (d)_________not always true. Many have (e)_______ their health to gain wealth, but later (f)___________ much of their wealth to regain health. Isn't that ironical? Again there are also a number of people who had (g)___________ high prices for possessing their present wealth. (a) possess; (b) claim; (c) brings; (d) is; (e) lost; (f) spent; (g) paid; (h) neglected; (i) lost; (j) neglected.

[Image]


A proverb goes that a man without an aim is a ship without a rudder. Likewise, a man without an aim (a)_________ reach his goal. He (b)________ in his way of life. So everyman should (c)_________ a definite aim. But nothing is more difficult than the choice of profession. Students (d)_________ it very difficult to choose a suitable__________ profession. Choosing profession becomes very difficult because there (e)__________ many paths and courses open to them. They should (f)__________ their aim according to the abilities they are (g)_________ with. All (h)_________ the same abilities and aptitude. Students may (i)________ their teachers who are able to (j)__________ their abilities.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Right form of verbs:

(a) cannot; (b) stumbles; (c) have; (d) find; (e) are; (f) fix; (g) endowed; (h) do not possess; (i) consult; (j) evaluate.

Complete the following text with right forms of the verbs given in the box :


[Image]


Social value (a) ---- to customs, beliefs, special practices and hamper reflect require & norms. It (b) ------- the culture of a nation. It (c) ------- great educative value in our life. In the past, people were very much conscious of (d) ------- social value in each and every walk of life. Earlier each and every person (e)---- very careful of social value. But at present our social value is in a great threat. Young people don't (f) ------ duly to their elders that results in social degradation. As a result, peace and order and decent life are greatly (g)------ So with a view to (h)------ peace and order in the society, social value is badly (i) ------Without social value we can't (j) ------decent, comfortable, happy and peaceful life.

Correct Answer:

Question #76 (ID: 481622)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
once my mother said to me who came to you my friend rafiq mom she asked what did he want i said his mother is ill he needs some money i have given him five hundred taka my mother said wonderful

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Once my mother said to me, "Who came to you?" "My friend, Rafiq, Mom." She asked, "What did he want?" I said, "His mother is ill. He needs some money. I have given him five hundred taka." My mother said, "Wonderful!"

Explanation:
This passage is converted into reported speech, so verbs shift back (present → past, past → past perfect where needed), pronouns are adjusted, and quotation marks are removed. Thus "his mother is ill; he needs some money; I have given him five hundred taka" becomes "his mother was ill; he needed some money; I had given him five hundred taka," and "my mother said wonderful" becomes "my mother said it was wonderful."

Question #83 (ID: 481629)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill in the gaps with suitable prepositions, articles and zero articles (a, an, the or x):

Washing hands regularly is (a)________ important activity. It keeps us safe (b)________ corona-virus. How you wash your hand is also very (c)________important. First, you have to wet your hands (d)_________clean, running water and apply soap. Then, rub your hands together with (e)_______ soap to create foam. Lather_________ the backs of your hands, (f)_________ your fingers and (g)_________your nails. Remember, you have to scrub your hands (h)_____ at least 20 seconds. After that rinse your hands well with clean and running water. Finally, dry your hands using (i)__________ clean towel or tissue paper. Learn the process (j) _________ washing hands and also educate your friends about it.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gap filling with articles or prepositions:

(a) an; (b) from; (c) x; (d) with; (e) the; (f) x; (g) x; (h) for; (i) a; (j) of.

Explanation:
Answers: (a) an; (b) from the coronavirus; (c) x (no article); (d) with; (e) x (no article); Lather — on; (f) between; (g) under; (h) for; (i) a; (j) of.

Explanation: Use [math]an[/math] before a vowel sound ("important") and [math]a[/math] before a singular countable noun ("a clean towel"); use zero article for uncountable/general nouns ("soap", "very important") or when no article is needed. Prepositions: [math]from[/math] shows protection against something, [math]with[/math] indicates means (water), [math]on/between/under[/math] show where to lather, [math]for[/math] expresses duration, and [math]of[/math] links "process" to "washing hands."

"Why are you putting the foods in your pocket, sir? Why don't you eat?" asked the nobleman.."I'm doing the right thing. My dress deserves these rich dishes," replied Sheikh Sa'adi. "I'm sorry. ("আপনি খাবারগুলো পকেটে রাখছেন কেন, স্যার? আপনি খান না কেন?” সম্ভ্রান্ত লোকটি জিজ্ঞেস করলেন। "আমি ঠিক কাজটি করছি। আমার পোশাক এই উন্নতমানের/দামি খাবারের যোগ্য," শেখ সা'দী উত্তর দিলেন। "আমি দুঃখিত। আমি বুঝতে পারছি না আপনি কী বলতে চাচ্ছেন," সম্ভ্রান্ত লোকটি বললেন।)

Explanation:
Each independent sentence needs an end punctuation (a period or a question mark), and direct speech should be enclosed in quotation marks with the question mark placed inside the quotes for a spoken question. Commas separate introductory words (e.g., "Look,") and clauses, and contractions require apostrophes (e.g., "didn't", "it's"), so the corrected text uses periods, commas, quotation marks, a question mark, and apostrophes accordingly.

Question #89 (ID: 481635)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Use punctuation marks where necessary in the following text:

Mainul Islam is a qualified farmer in Naogaon He lives in his village with his two brothers When he was asked What makes you decide to stay here in this village He replied Look its true that we could leave this village for a city life But it didnt attract us

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Punctuation:

Mainul Islam is a qualified farmer in Naogaon. He lives in his village with his two brothers. When he was asked, "What make you decide to stay here in this village?" He replied, "Look, it's true that we could leave this village for a city life, but it didn't attract us." (মইনুল ইসলাম নওগাঁর একজন দক্ষ কৃষক। তিনি তার দুই ভাইকে নিয়ে গ্রামে থাকেন। যখন তাকে জিজ্ঞেস করা হল, "কী আপনাকে এই গ্রামে থাকতে সিদ্ধান্ত নেওয়ায়?" তিনি উত্তর দিলেন, "দেখুন, এটা সত্য যে আমরা শহরের জীবনের জন্য এই গ্রাম ছেড়ে যেতে পারতাম, কিন্তু এটি আমাদের আকর্ষণ করেনি।")

Explanation:
Punctuation shows sentence boundaries and marks quoted speech: place a comma after the introductory clause ("When he was asked,") and enclose the spoken question in quotation marks with a question mark inside ("What makes you decide to stay here in this village?"). Also put a comma after the reporting verb before the reply, use a comma after "Look" and apostrophes in contractions ("it's", "didn't"), and end the reply with a period.

why dont you attend classes regularly the teacher said to the boy you cannot expect good result unless you attend classes be regular in class

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:

Explanation:
The teacher asked the boy why he did not attend classes regularly, told him that he could not expect good results unless he attended classes, and advised him to be regular in class. Question #118 (ID: 481619)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
the man said to me where are you going i am going to school said i did you go to school yesterday no i replied why didn’t you go i was very busy said i

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The man said to me. "Where are you going?" "I am going to school," said I. "Did you go to school yesterday?" "No," I replied. "Why didn't you go?" "I was very busy," said I.

Explanation:
In reported speech we backshift tenses, change pronouns and keep question word order as a statement. So "Where are you going?" becomes "He asked me where I was going," "I am going to school" → "I said (that) I was going to school," "Did you go to school yesterday?" → "He asked if I had gone to school yesterday," "No" → "I replied that I had not," "Why didn’t you go?" → "He asked why I hadn’t gone," and "I was very busy" → "I said (that) I had been very busy."

Question #119 (ID: 481620)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
bangladesh is a small country with a population of about sixteen crores she can hardly make headway so we should work hard to keep pace with the rest of the world

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Bangladesh is a small country. With a population of about sixteen crore, she can hardly make headway. So, we should work hard to keep pace with the rest of the world.

Explanation:
The sentence has capitalization, punctuation and clarity issues: begin with a capital "Bangladesh", avoid a run-on by separating clauses, and prefer the neutral pronoun "it" in formal writing. Also express the population clearly (e.g., "about sixteen crore" or "about 160 million"). Corrected example: "Bangladesh is a small country with a population of about sixteen crore (about 160 million); it can hardly make headway, so we should work hard to keep pace with the rest of the world."

Question #120 (ID: 481621)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
the teacher said to the boy where are you going now i am going to school said the boy did you go to school yesterday no the boy replied why did you not go i was suffering from fever said the boy

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The teacher said to the boy, "Where are you going now?" "I am going to school," said the boy. "Did you go to school yesterday?" "No," the boy replied. "Why did you not go?" "I was suffering from fever, said the boy.

Explanation:
Because the reporting verb is in the past ("said"), all present and past tenses backshift: "are going" becomes "was going" and "I was suffering" becomes "he had been suffering." Yes/no questions are introduced with if/whether and past simple ("Did you go yesterday?") becomes past perfect ("if/whether he had gone the day before"), and time words change ("now" → "then", "yesterday" → "the day before").

Question #121 (ID: 481552)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
“How lovely the doll is! I’ll buy it,” said Mona. “No, it is not durable. Tomorrow we’ll visit another village fair. Then you can buy another doll. Let’s go now,” said mother. “You must buy me a good doll,” said Mona. “Yes,” replied mother.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Mona exclaimed with joy that the doll was very lovely. She told her mother that she would buy it. Mother replied in the negative saying that it was not durable. She added that the next day they would visit another village fair and then she (Mona) could buy another doll. Saying that mother proposed to her (Mona) that they should go then. Then Mona told her mother that she had to buy her (Mona) a good doll. Mother agreed with her.

Explanation:
The correct indirect-speech version uses backshifting of tenses, changes exclamations to "exclaimed" or "said" and shifts time/place words (e.g., "tomorrow" → "the next day"). For example, Mona’s “How lovely the doll is! I’ll buy it,” becomes Mona exclaimed that the doll was lovely and that she would buy it; Mother’s “Tomorrow we’ll visit another village fair” becomes she said they would visit the next day and urged them to go then. Imperatives like “Let’s go now” become suggestions or urgings (she told them to go), and direct requests like “You must buy me a good doll” become Mona insisted that her mother must/should buy her a good doll, with the short reply “Yes” reported as agreement.

Question:
The police officer said to Mita, “How can I help you?” Mita replied, “While I was coming home alone by a taxi last night, two snatchers rode into my taxi.” “Did they snatch anything from you?” “Yes sir, they took away my cell phone and some money,” said Mita. “Let me record a complaint,” said the police officer.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The police officer asked Mita how he could help her. Mita replied that while she had been going home alone by a taxi the previous night, two snatchers had ridden into her taxi. Then the police officer again asked her if they had snatched anything from her. Mita respectfully replied in the affirmative and said that they had taken away her cell phone and some money. The police officer told her that he might be allowed to record a complaint.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এখানে "Let me record a complaint" একটি প্রস্তাব/প্রস্তাবনা নির্দেশ করে; reported speech-এ এমন প্রস্তাব প্রকাশ করতে আমরা সাধারণত "offered to" বা "said (that) he would" ব্যবহার করি। তাই সঠিক রূপ হবে: "The police officer offered to record a complaint" বা "The police officer said (that) he would record a complaint" — কারণ প্রথম পুরুষের "let me" রিপোর্টেড স্পিচে প্রস্তাব হিসেবে বদলে যায়।

Question:
delete hobe

“What’s your programme after the examination?” asked Hira. Mira said, “I’ve not decided. Can you suggest any?” “Let us go on a picnic,” said Hira. “What an excellent idea it is!” said Mira.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:

"I've not decided" becomes "she had not decided," and "Can you suggest any?" becomes "she asked if Hira could suggest any." Commands and exclamations change to reporting verbs: Hira suggested that they go on a picnic, and Mira exclaimed that it was an excellent idea.

Question #124 (ID: 481555)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Rosamond said to her mother, “What is it, Mum? I didn’t want this black thing and the terrible smell.” Mother said, “I don’t know, my dear. “Rosamond again said to her mother, “But what shall I do with it?” Mother said, “I can’t tell.” “Okay, Mum, I must pour it out and fill the jar with fresh water.”

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Addressing her mother as Mum, Rosamond asked her what it was. She also (R) said that she (R) had not wanted that black thing and the terrible smell. In reply mother told her affectionately that she (M) didn't know it. But Rosamond again asked her mother what she (R) would do with that. Mother again replied that she couldn't tell. Rosamond said that it was okay and told her mother endearingly that she (R) had to pour it out and fill the jar with fresh water.

Explanation:
The black thing and terrible smell show the water or its contents are contaminated or rotten, so keeping it could be unsafe or unpleasant. Since the mother cannot identify or advise about the contamination, Rosamond’s decision to pour it out and refill the jar with fresh water is the sensible, hygienic choice.

Question #125 (ID: 481556)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
“Hello rickshawpuller, will you go?” said I. “Where?” said the rickshawpuller. “I want to go the railway station.” “I may go, if you pay me 200 taka.” said the rickshawpuller.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Drawing the attention of the rickshawpuller I asked him if he would go. The rickshawpuller asked me where I would go. I replied that I wanted to go to the railway station. The rickshawpuller told me that he might go, if I paid him 200 taka.

Explanation:
The rickshaw‑puller asks “Where?” to learn the destination, and when told “railway station” he replies he will go only if paid 200 taka—so the correct answer (that he demanded fare) follows directly from his conditional reply. This teaches reading dialogue by noting questions that ask for information and responses that state conditions or requests.

Question #126 (ID: 481557)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
“May I come in, Sir?” said the guardian. “Yes, come in, please”, said the Headmaster. The guardian said, “We. all the guardians along with you must do something for the betterment of our children. They are losing their morality”. The Headmaster said, “Let’s plan something for their betterment.”

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The guardian politely asked the headmaster if he (g) might go in. The headmaster replied in the affirmative and requested him (g) to come in. The guardian said that they, all the guardians along with him (H) had to do something for the betterment of their children. He (g) also said that they were losing their morality. The headmaster suggested that they should plan something for their betterment.

Explanation:
When converting to reported speech we shift tense and change forms: a question like “May I come in?” becomes the guardian asking if he [math]might[/math] come in (because [math]may[/math] → [math]might[/math] in indirect speech), and an imperative like “Yes, come in, please” becomes the headmaster telling him to come in (imperative → told/requested + to‑infinitive). The guardian’s remark about guardians doing something is reported as him saying that all the guardians, along with the headmaster, must do something for the children’s betterment and that the children were losing their morality (present progressive → past progressive). “Let’s plan something” is reported as the headmaster suggesting that they plan (or should plan) something.
