Question #257 (ID: 481425)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The foods that we eat can be divided into six kinds (a) — what substances they contain and (b) — benefits they do to us. Fish, meat, peas and milk provide us with protein (c) — builds our body and helps us grow. (d) — we do not take all these, we cannot grow well. Vitamins and mineral salts protect us from diseases (e) — keep us fit for work.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) according to; (b) what; (c) which/that; (d) If; (e) and.

Explanation:
Explanation:
ক ও খ — "according to" ব্যবহার করা হয় কারণ খাবারগুলোকে নির্দিষ্ট ভিত্তি অনুযায়ী ভাগ করা হচ্ছে (কী থাকে এবং কী সুবিধা দেয়), তাই একই বাক্যগঠনের জন্য একই শব্দ দরকার।  
গ — "which" দুইটি অংশকে জোড়ার মাধ্যমে প্রটিনকে বর্ণনা করে: প্রটিনই আমাদের দেহ গঠনে সাহায্য করে।  
ঘ — "If" শর্ত বোঝায়; যদি আমরা এসব না নিই তাহলে ভালভাবে বেড়ে উঠতে পারব না।  
ঙ — "and" দুটি ক্রিয়ার ফলাফলকে সংযুক্ত করে: ভিটামিন ও খনিজ লবণ রোগ থেকে রক্ষা করে এবং আমাদের কাজের জন্য সুস্থ রাখে।

Question #258 (ID: 481373)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following sentences:

(a) "Health is wealth"

(b) Everybody should realize this truth to.

(c) If we follow the rules of health

(d) One can keep oneself safe by

(e) Immune system can be developed by

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) "Health is wealth" is a saying/proverb. ("স্বাস্থ্যই সম্পদ" একটি প্রবাদ/প্রবচন।)

(b) Everybody should realize this truth to enjoy a happy life. (সুখী জীবন উপভোগ করার জন্য প্রত্যেকেরই এই সত্য উপলব্ধি করা উচিত।)

(c) If we follow the rules of health, we will be healthy and wealthy. (আমরা যদি স্বাস্থ্যবিধি মেনে চলি তাহলে আমরা সুস্থ ও সম্পদশালী হব।)

(d) One can keep oneself safe by maintaining the rules of health. (স্বাস্থ্যবিধি বজায় রেখে যে কেউ নিজেকে নিরাপদ রাখতে পারে।)

(e) Immune system can be developed by practising health rules. (স্বাস্থ্যবিধি মেনে চলার মাধ্যমে রোগ প্রতিরোধ ব্যবস্থা গড়ে তোলা যায়।)

Explanation:
(a) Health is wealth.
Explanation: Good health allows a person to work, enjoy life, and achieve goals, so it is more valuable than material possessions.

(b) Everybody should realize this truth too.
Explanation: When people accept the importance of health, they are more likely to adopt healthy habits and prevent illness.

(c) If we follow the rules of health, we can prevent many diseases and lead a better life.
Explanation: Healthy practices (hygiene, diet, exercise) reduce risk factors and keep the body functioning well.

(d) One can keep oneself safe by maintaining cleanliness, eating a balanced diet, exercising regularly, and getting enough sleep.
Explanation: These actions lower exposure to infection and strengthen the body’s ability to resist disease.

(e) Immune system can be developed by proper nutrition, regular exercise, adequate sleep, and vaccination.
Explanation: Nutrients, rest, physical activity, and vaccines support immune-cell production and improve the body’s defense against infections.

Question #259 (ID: 481374)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the sentences of the following text by using conditionals, infinitives, gerunds and participles:

(a) If we invest in girls' education________.

(b) ________ is not a waste.

(c) ________have higher income potential than those who are uneducated and unskilled.

(d) Also, educated mothers are very careful in_________.

(e) Therefore, we should try our best__________.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) If we invest in girls' education, our country will be benefited. (মেয়েদের শিক্ষায় বিনিয়োগ করলে আমাদের দেশ উপকৃত হবে।)

(b) Investing in education for girls is not a waste. (মেয়েদের শিক্ষায় বিনিয়োগ করা কোনো অপচয় নয়।)

(c) The educated girls have higher income potential than those who are uneducated and unskilled. (অশিক্ষিত এবং অদক্ষ মেয়েদের তুলনায় শিক্ষিত মেয়েদের আয়ের সম্ভাবনা বেশি।)

(d) Also, educated mothers are very careful in educating their children. (এছাড়াও, শিক্ষিত মায়েরা তাদের সন্তানদের শিক্ষিত করার ক্ষেত্রে খুব যত্নশীল।)

(e) Therefore, we should try our best to educate our girls. (অতএব, আমাদের মেয়েদের শিক্ষিত করার জন্য আমাদের যথাসাধ্য চেষ্টা করা উচিত।)

Explanation:
(a) If we invest in girls' education, they will contribute to national development.
(b) Investing in girls' education is not a waste.
(c) Educated and skilled women have higher income potential than those who are uneducated and unskilled.
(d) Also, educated mothers are very careful in raising their children.
(e) Therefore, we should try our best to provide equal educational opportunities for girls.

Explanation:
These choices show correct grammatical forms: (a) uses a first conditional to link investment and result; (b) uses a gerund phrase as the subject; (c) uses a plural noun phrase to compare groups; (d) follows the preposition "in" with a gerund to name an ongoing activity; (e) uses an infinitive to express purpose or obligation. Each form fits the meaning and grammatical role required in the sentence.

Question #260 (ID: 481375)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following sentences:

(a) If the sky is cloudy,___________.

(b) ____________which should be given up.

(c) Man is curious___________.

(d) If I had seen him,____________.

(e) I saw a bird____________.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) If the sky is cloudy; you will not go out. (আকাশ মেঘলা হলে বাইরে যাবে না।)

(b) Eating junk food is a habit which should be given up. (মুখোরোচক খাবার খাওয়া একটি অভ্যাস যা ত্যাগ করা উচিত।)

(c) Man is curious to know the unknown. (মানুষ অজানাকে জানতে আগ্রহী।)

(d) If I had seen him, I would have told him the matter. (আমি যদি তাকে দেখতে পেতাম তবে আমি তাকে বিষয়টি বলতাম।)

(e) I saw a bird flying in the sky. (আমি একটি পাখিকে আকাশে উড়তে দেখলাম।)

Explanation:
(a) If the sky is cloudy, it will probably rain.
Explanation: This is a real conditional about weather, so we use present tense in the if-clause and "will" + base verb in the main clause to show a likely future result.

(b) There are some habits which should be given up.
Explanation: "There are some…" introduces existence, and the relative clause "which should be given up" specifies those habits that ought to be abandoned.

(c) Man is curious by nature.
Explanation: "By nature" is a fixed phrase expressing a general truth about people, so this sentence states a habitual/characteristic quality.

(d) If I had seen him, I would have spoken to him.
Explanation: This is a third conditional (unreal past): "If" + past perfect in the if-clause and "would have" + past participle in the result clause to show an action that did not happen.

(e) I saw a bird flying.
Explanation: Simple past "saw" reports a past observation, and the present participle "flying" describes what the bird was doing at that time.

Question #261 (ID: 481376)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following sentences using conditionals, infinitives, gerunds and participles.

(a) A cobbler was happy to________.

(b) He had a neighbour__________.

(c) The neighbour wanted to help him by____________.

(d) _____________, the cobbler lost happiness.

(e) But if he had not taken the money from his neighbour,___________.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) A cobbler was happy to lead a simple life. (এক মুচি সহজসরল জীবনযাপন করতে পেরে খুশি ছিল।)

(b) He had a neighbour who was very helpful. (তার একজন প্রতিবেশী ছিল যে খুবই সহায়ক ছিল।)

(c) The neighbour wanted to help him by donating him some money. (এই প্রতিবেশী তাকে কিছু অর্থ দান করে সাহায্য করতে চেয়েছিল।)

(d) Having taken the money from the neighbour, the cobbler lost happiness. (প্রতিবেশীর কাছ থেকে টাকা নিয়ে মুচি সুখ হারিয়ে ফেলেছিল।)

(e) But if he had not taken the money from his neighbour, he could have lived a happy life. (কিন্তু যদি সে তার প্রতিবেশীর কাছ থেকে টাকা না নিত তাহলে সে সুখী জীবনযাপন করতে পারতো।)

Explanation:
Answers:
(a) A cobbler was happy to earn his living by repairing shoes.
(b) He had a neighbour willing to help him.
(c) The neighbour wanted to help him by lending him some money.
(d) After receiving the money, the cobbler lost his happiness.
(e) But if he had not taken the money from his neighbour, he would still have been happy.

Explanation:
These choices follow common grammatical patterns: (a) uses the infinitive after "happy to" to show purpose or result; (b) uses "willing to" (an adjective + infinitive/participle) to describe the neighbour; (c) uses the gerund after "by" ("by lending") to show the means of helping; (d) uses a participle/gerund phrase ("After receiving") to indicate the time/cause; and (e) uses the third conditional ("If he had not…, he would have…") to express an unreal past result.

Question #262 (ID: 481377)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following statements:

(a) "Industry is the key to success"_________.

(b) If you want to shine in life,___________.

(c) By working hard, one_________.

(d) A hardworking student is sure_________.

(e) It is high time for us to_________.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) "Industry is the key to success" is a saying. ("পরিশ্রম সফলতার চাবিকাঠি" একটি প্রবাদ।)

(b) If you want to shine in life, you have to work hard. (তুমি যদি জীবনে উন্নতি লাভ করতে চাও তবে তোমাকে কঠোর পরিশ্রম করতে হবে।)

(c) By working hard, one can prosper in life. (কঠোর পরিশ্রম করে একজন ব্যক্তি জীবনে উন্নতি করতে পারে।)

(d) A hardworking student is sure of his success. (কঠোর পরিশ্রমী একজন শিক্ষার্থী তার সফলতার ব্যাপারে নিশ্চিত।)

(e) It is high time for us to work hard. (আমাদের কঠোর পরিশ্রম করার এখনই উপযুক্ত সময়।)

Explanation:
Explanation:

(a) "Industry is the key to success" is a proverb. This sentence states a general truth that hard work (industry) leads to success.

(b) If you want to shine in life, you must work hard. "Shine" here means succeed or stand out, and effort is the means to achieve that.

(c) By working hard, one can achieve success. Hard work produces results, so effort leads to accomplishment.

(d) A hardworking student is sure to succeed. Regular effort improves understanding and results, making success likely.

(e) It is high time for us to take action. "High time" implies urgency, so we must start doing something now rather than delaying.

Question #263 (ID: 481378)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following sentences (using conditionals, gerund, infinitive, participle):

(a) If you eat a balanced diet,___________.

(b) __________ I would join the party,

(c) ___________ is a good exercise.

(d) His syllabus is___________.

(e) ___________ is a great sin.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) If you eat balanced diet, you can enjoy a happy life, (যদি তুমি সুষম খাবার খাও তাহলে তুমি সুখী জীবন উপভোগ করতে পারবে।)

(b) If I had time, I would join the party. (আমার যদি সময় থাকতো তাহলে আমি পার্টিতে যোগ দিতাম।)

(c) Walking is a good exercise. (হাঁটা একটি ভালো ব্যায়াম।) (d) His syllabus is incomplete. (তার পাঠ্যসূচি অসম্পূর্ণ।)

(e) Telling a lie is a great sin. (মিথ্যা বলা মহাপাপ।)

Explanation:
(a) If you eat a balanced diet, you will stay healthy.  
This is a first conditional: the if-clause uses present simple ("eat") for a real possibility, and the main clause uses "will" for the result.

(b) If I were invited, I would join the party.  
This is a second conditional for an unreal or unlikely situation: use the past subjunctive ("were") in the if-clause and "would" in the main clause.

(c) Walking is a good exercise.  
"Walking" is a gerund (verb+ing) functioning as a noun and the subject of the sentence.

(d) His syllabus is well designed.  
"Designed" is a past participle used adjectivally (with "well") to describe the syllabus.

(e) Lying is a great sin.  
"Lying" is a gerund naming the action and acting as the subject, which is common when talking about general moral statements.

Question #264 (ID: 481379)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the following sentences:

(a) I feel like__________.

(b) Babies do not know___________.

(c) I saw a beggar___________.

(d) Were I a rich man,____________.

(e) If you do not work hard,___________.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completing Sentences:

(a) I feel like going for a walk in the evening. (আমার সন্ধ্যায় হাঁটতে ইচ্ছে করছে।)

(b) Babies do not know how to read and write, (শিশুরা পড়তে ও লিখতে জানে না।)

(c) I saw a begger begging on the street, (আমি একজন ভিক্ষুককে রাস্তায় ভিক্ষা করতে দেখলাম।)

(d) Were I a rich man, I would help the poor. (আমি যদি ধনী হতাম তাহলে আমি গরিবদের সাহায্য করতাম।)

(e) If you do not work hard, you cannot shine in life, (তুমি যদি কঠোর পরিশ্রম না করো তবে তুমি জীবনে উন্নতি করতে পারবে না।)

Explanation:
(a) I feel like going for a walk.
Explanation: "Feel like" is followed by a gerund to express a desire or inclination, so "going" (gerund) is correct.

(b) Babies do not know right from wrong.
Explanation: This noun phrase shows that infants haven’t developed moral judgment yet; "do not know" correctly takes the noun phrase "right from wrong."

(c) I saw a beggar sitting by the road.
Explanation: With verbs of perception like "saw," use object + present participle to describe the action you observed ("saw someone sitting").

(d) Were I a rich man, I would travel the world.
Explanation: This is an inverted subjunctive conditional (equivalent to "If I were...") used for hypothetical situations; the main clause uses "would."

(e) If you do not work hard, you will fail the exam.
Explanation: This is a first conditional: present simple in the "if" clause with "will" in the main clause to express a likely future consequence.

Question #265 (ID: 481380)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2020 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) No sooner had we reached the school —.

(b) Unless you study attentively —.

(c) Scarcely had the party begun —.

(d) If I had known his mobile number, —.

(e) Work hard provided that —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation:
(a) No sooner had we reached the school —.
The correct continuation uses "than" with inversion, e.g. "No sooner had we reached the school than the bell rang." This structure (No sooner + auxiliary + subject + past participle ... than ...) shows one action immediately followed another.

(b) Unless you study attentively —.
"Unless" means "if not," so the main clause normally uses the future: "Unless you study attentively, you will fail the exam." It expresses a negative condition: success depends on studying.

(c) Scarcely had the party begun —.
This pairs with "when" (or "before") and uses inversion, e.g. "Scarcely had the party begun when it started to rain." "Scarcely/hardly ... when" indicates one event happened immediately after another.

(d) If I had known his mobile number, —.
This is a third‑conditional (past unreal): "If I had known his mobile number, I would have called him." Form: If + past perfect, ... would have + past participle (an unreal past result).

(e) Work hard provided that —.
"Provided that" means "on condition that," so complete with a condition: "Work hard provided that you want to succeed." It sets a requirement — you should work hard only if that condition holds (or it explains the reason/condition for the advice).

Question #266 (ID: 481386)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2020 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) I am looking for Raihan. If I had seen him, —.

(b) Shila seemed upset. She talked as if —.

(c) Yesterday we were at our office. Scarcely had we finished our duty —.

(d) We are not free from danger. Danger often comes where —.

(e) Restless life is risky. We have to take rest —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
(a) If I had seen him, I would have told you.
Explanation: This is a past unreal (third) conditional: "If" + past perfect ("had seen") with "would have" + past participle to show a hypothetical past action that did not happen.

(b) She talked as if she were upset.
Explanation: After "as if" to describe an unreal or hypothetical state we use the subjunctive "were" (even with past narration), so "as if she were upset" fits the meaning that she appeared upset.

(c) Scarcely had we finished our duty when the bell rang.
Explanation: "Scarcely... when" shows one action immediately followed another; inversion ("Scarcely had we...") is required after "scarcely" in this structure.

(d) Danger often comes where we least expect it.
Explanation: This is a common idiom meaning danger appears unexpectedly; "where we least expect it" completes the thought naturally and idiomatically.

(e) We have to take rest from time to time.
Explanation: "From time to time" (or "occasionally") expresses the idea of taking periodic rest, which matches the warning that a restless life is risky.

Question #267 (ID: 481387)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Where there is a will, —.

(b) If a man does not work hard, —.

(c) As the people of Bangladesh are hard-working, —.

(d) But now she has made a remarkable development in her GDP —.

(e) So, it is our bounden duty to —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
(a) "Where there is a will, there is a way." — This proverb means that firm determination leads people to find solutions; if someone truly wants to achieve something, they will overcome obstacles.

(b) "If a man does not work hard, he will not succeed." — Success generally follows effort; without persistent hard work one cannot expect to achieve goals or rewards.

(c) "As the people of Bangladesh are hard-working, the country is developing steadily." — A diligent workforce raises productivity and investment, so collective hard work contributes directly to national development.

(d) "But now she has made a remarkable development in her GDP, indicating significant economic growth." — An increasing GDP reflects higher production, incomes and investment, so a notable GDP rise shows the economy is expanding.

(e) "So, it is our bounden duty to work for the country's progress and safeguard its achievements." — Citizens’ responsibility is to contribute through hard work, honesty and protection of resources so that development is sustained.

Question #268 (ID: 481389)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) We should keep in mind that —.

(b) If we are not healthy —.

(c) We must eat balanced diet so that —.

(d) We should wear socks and shoes when —.

(e) Nobody likes a man who —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ক এই বাক্য শুরুটি কোনো গুরুত্বপূর্ণ কথা মনে করিয়ে দেওয়ার জন্য ব্যবহৃত হয়, তাই শেষ অংশে এমন একটি সাধারণ সত্য বা সতর্কতা দেওয়া উচিত যা মনে রাখা প্রয়োজন।  

খ এখানে একটি শর্তসূচক বাক্য রয়েছে — শর্ত পূরণ না হলে তার ফল হয়; সুতরাং শেষাংশে শর্ত অনুযায়ী ফলাফল (যেমন কাজ করতে না পারা বা ডাক্তারের কাছে যাওয়া) থাকা উচিত।  

গ "so that" হলো উদ্দেশ্য বা ফল প্রকাশ করার詞, তাই শেষাংশে এমন ফল দেওয়া উচিত যা ব্যালান্সড ডায়েট খাওয়ার উদ্দেশ্য হিসেবে মানায় (যেমন সুস্থ থাকা বা প্রয়োজনীয় পুষ্টি পাওয়া)।  

ঘ এখানে পরিস্থিতি বা অবস্থান নির্দেশ করা হচ্ছে—জুতা ও মোজা পরার কারণ সুরক্ষা বা আরাম; তাই শেষাংশে বাইরে চলাচল বা ঠাণ্ডা/কঠিন জায়গায় হাঁটার মত পরিস্থিতি উল্লেখ করা উচিত।  

ঙ এই বাক্যে একটি সম্পর্কবাচক ক্লজ আছে যা মানুষের অপ্রিয় গুণ বর্ণনা করে; তাই শেষাংশে এমন একটা নেতিবাচক গুণ (রূক্ষতা, মিথ্যাচার, স্বার্থপরতা ইত্যাদি) দেওয়া উচিত যা মানুষকে অপ্রিয় করে তোলে।

Question #270 (ID: 481392)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) The mango is a fruit which —.

(b) It is so delicious that —.

(c) Rajshahi is the place where —.

(d) If you visit Rajshahi, Bogura and Dinajpur —.

(e) People of this area produce a huge amount of mangoes and —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation:

(a) The mango is a fruit which is rich in vitamins. — "which" introduces a relative clause giving more information about "fruit."

(b) It is so delicious that everyone likes it. — "so ... that" expresses a result; "that" introduces the result clause (everyone likes it).

(c) Rajshahi is the place where many mangoes are grown. — "where" links the noun "place" to a clause describing what happens in that place (in which many mangoes are grown).

(d) If you visit Rajshahi, Bogura and Dinajpur, you will see large mango orchards. — A real conditional: present tense in the "if" clause plus "will" in the main clause shows a likely future result.

(e) People of this area produce a huge amount of mangoes and export them. — "and" connects two related actions (producing and exporting) to complete the idea.

Question #271 (ID: 481393)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: All Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) It is English which —.

(b) But most of the students don’t know how —.

(c) If a student wants to do well in English —.

(d) Unless he/she practices it, —.

(e) It is high time —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) It is English which can help us for global communication .

(b) But most of the students don't know how to learn English .

(c) If a student wants to do well in English s/he has to practise it .

(d) Unless s/he practises it, it will be difficult for her/him to learn it .

(e) It is high time we had a sound knowledge of English .

Explanation:
(a) This is a cleft construction where "which" introduces a relative clause referring back to "English"; complete it with a clause like "which I enjoy most" so the relative pronoun has a verb and object.  
(b) After "how" use an indirect-question or an infinitival phrase: e.g., "how to study" or "how they can improve"; for instructions prefer "how to + base verb."  
(c) This begins a first‑conditional idea: use "If + present simple, ... will/should/can + base verb" (e.g., "If a student wants to do well in English, he/she should practise regularly").  
(d) "Unless" means "if not," so follow it with present simple and a result clause (often future): e.g., "Unless he/she practices it, he/she won't improve."  
(e) After "It is high time" use a past tense/subjunctive to show something should already happen: e.g., "It is high time you started working harder."

Question #272 (ID: 481394)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Books are our best friends because —

(b) A man who reads books regularly —

(c) By reading books —

(d) We can learn moral values —

(e) We should inspire the students —

Options:

Solution:
(a) Books are our best friends because we always find them in our weal and woe .

(b) A man who reads books regularly, can enrich himself with knowledge .

(c) By reading books we can learn many things necessary for us .

(d) We can learn moral values by reading books .

(e) We should inspire the students to read books .

ক বই আমাদের শ্রেষ্ঠ বন্ধু কারণ এগুলো নিরবচ্ছিন্নভাবে জ্ঞান, নির্দেশনা ও নতুন দৃষ্টিভঙ্গি দেয় যা জীবনে সাহায্য করে।

ঘ আমরা নৈতিক মূল্যবোধ বই থেকে শিখি কারণ গল্প ও চরিত্রের মাধ্যমে সঠিক-বাতিল, সহানুভূতি ও নৈতিক সিদ্ধান্ত বোঝানো হয়।  
ঙ আমরা ছাত্র-ছাত্রীদের বই পড়ার অনুপ্রেরণা দেওয়া উচিত যাতে তারা নিয়মিত জ্ঞানার্জন, শৃঙ্খলা ও সমালোচনামূলক চিন্তা গড়ে তুলতে পারে।

Question #273 (ID: 481395)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) There goes a proverb that — .

(b) Though lost wealth can be regained by hard work, lost time — .

(c) Time is so valuable that — .

(d) Those who — cannot shine in life.

(e) —, you must be successful.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) There goes a proverb that time and tide wait for none .

(b) Though lost wealth can be regained by hard work, lost time can never be regained .

(c) Time is so valuable that we should not waste it .

(d) Those who idle away their time , cannot shine in life.

(e) If you make the best use of time , you must be successful.

Explanation:
(a) "There goes a proverb that time and tide wait for none" — This proverb is correct because time moves on regardless of our wishes; it teaches that we must act promptly since opportunities do not pause.

(b) "Though lost wealth can be regained by hard work, lost time cannot be regained" — Time is irreversible, so once it is gone it cannot be recovered, which is why we should value and use it wisely.

(c) "Time is so valuable that we must not waste a single moment" — This emphasizes that every moment has potential value for work or learning, so wasting time reduces our chances of progress.

(d) "Those who waste time cannot shine in life" — Habitual procrastination or idleness prevents steady effort and skill-building, so such people miss the consistent work needed for success.

(e) "Use your time well, and you must be successful" — Good time management increases productivity and creates opportunities, making success far more likely.

Question #274 (ID: 481396)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) It is said that —.

(b) In youth the mind is soft that —.

(c) If we lose the morning hours of life —.

(d) We will reap good harvest —.

(e) On the other hand, if we remain lazy —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) It is said that youth is the best part of our life .

(b) In youth the mind is so soft that we can shape it according to our wish .

(c) If we lose the morning hours of life, we can't reach the goal of life .

(d) We will reap good harvest if we sow the good seeds with proper nursing .

(e) On the other hand, if we remain lazy, we must suffer in the long run .

Explanation:
(a) The correct completion is a proverb about early rising and disciplined habits: it says that regular, orderly routines (like rising early) promote health, efficiency and success. This is right because habits formed by discipline produce better physical and mental results over time.

(b) The right idea is that a young mind is pliable and easily shaped by teaching and example. That’s why education and good influence in youth have a lasting effect on character and behaviour.

(c) The sentence means that once the early, most productive years are wasted they cannot be recovered. It’s correct because time is irreversible, so losing youthful opportunities reduces future potential.

(d) This completes the cause–effect idea: if we sow good work or habits, we will reap a good harvest (good results). It’s true because effort and wise choices tend to produce corresponding positive outcomes.

(e) The contrast shows that laziness brings failure or loss of opportunities. This is right because inactivity and neglect prevent progress, so one cannot expect good results without effort.

Question #275 (ID: 481397)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Cricket is a game —.

(b) Boys and girls of our country —.

(c) Though cricket is a costly game, —-.

(d) Bangladesh is a test playing country —.

(e) — to upgrade the standard.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Cricket is a game which is full of thrill and excitement .

(b) Boys and girls of our country are very fond of cricket .

(c) Though cricket is a costly game, it is played all over the world .

(d) Bangladesh is a test playing country but its standard is not so high .

(e) Our players are trying hard to upgrade the standard.

Explanation:
(a) "Cricket is a game of skill."  
It requires batting, bowling, fielding techniques and tactical judgment, so "of skill" correctly describes its nature.

(b) "Boys and girls of our country play cricket."  
Cricket is very popular among both boys and girls in schools and communities, so "play cricket" completes the idea.

(c) "Though cricket is a costly game, many people play it."  
Despite the expense of formal equipment, informal street or backyard cricket and strong popularity lead many people to play.

(d) "Bangladesh is a test playing country now."  
Bangladesh gained Test status (in 2000) and participates in Test matches, so "now" correctly indicates its current status.

(e) "Steps should be taken to upgrade the standard."  
To raise the level of cricket, planned actions like better coaching, facilities and training are needed, so "steps should be taken" fits.

Question #276 (ID: 481398)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Slum dwellers are so poor —.

(b) As they live there in an inhuman condition, —.

(c) Although they do hard labour from dawn to dusk, —.

(d) Come forward to help them lest —.

(e) Only then they will be able to —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Slum dwellers are so poor that they often have to starve.

(b) As they live there in an inhuman condition, they suffer from various diseases .

(c) Although they do hard labour from dawn to dusk, they cannot earn much .

(d) Come forward to help them lest they should/might be poorer .

(e) Only then they will be able to lead a modest life .

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক "তারা এতই গরীব যে মৌলিক চাহিদাও পূরণ করতে পারে না।" — কারণ 'so ... that' কাঠামোর বাংলা প্রকাশে 'এত ... যে' ব্যবহার করে পরিণতি বোঝানো যায়।  
খ "সেখানে তারা অমানবিক অবস্থায় থাকায় অসুস্থতা ও অপর্যাপ্ত পরিষ্কার-পরিচ্ছন্নতার শিকার হয়।" — 'As' এখানে কারণ দেখায়, তাই 'কারণ/এতে' ধরনের অনুবাদ উপযুক্ত।  
গ "তারা ভোর থেকে সন্ধ্যা পর্যন্ত কঠোর পরিশ্রম করলেও মজুরি খুবই কম পায়।" — 'Although' বিরোধসূচক, তাই 'তবুও/তবৎ' জনিত বিরোধ নির্দেশ করে এমন রূপ ব্যবহার করা হয়।  
ঘ "আমরা তাদের সাহায্যে এগিয়ে আসবো, নতুবা তারা আরও দারিদ্র্যে পতিত হবে।" — 'lest' নেতিবাচক ফল এড়াতে বলে; বাংলা অনুবাদে 'নতুবা/নাহলে' যথোপযুক্ত।  
ঙ "শুধু তখনই তারা স্বনির্ভর হয়ে জীবনের মান উন্নত করতে পারবে।" — 'Only then' একটি শর্ত-ফল সম্পর্ক দেখায়, তাই ফল হিসেবে স্বনির্ভরতা বলা যায়।

Question #277 (ID: 481399)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Five years have passed since —

(b) Hardly had the assembly began —

(c) — lest you should miss the plane.

(d) Danger often comes —

(e) The lady speaks as if —

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Five years have passed since I saw you last .

(b) Hardly had the assembly begun when an unknown person entered the assembly house .

(c) Drive fast/Hurry up/Walk fast/Run fast . lest you should miss the plane.

(d) Danger often comes where it is leared.

(e) The lady speaks as if she knew everything well .

Explanation:
(a) Five years have passed since I left school.  
Explanation: With a present-perfect time span like "have passed," "since" introduces a point in the past, so we use simple past ("I left") to mark the starting point.

(b) Hardly had the assembly begun when the principal arrived.  
Explanation: "Hardly" requires inversion with the past perfect ("had begun" — past participle), and "when" links the shortly following event.

(c) Leave early, lest you should miss the plane.  
Explanation: "Lest" expresses prevention and is followed formally by "should" + base verb ("should miss") to show what to avoid.

(d) Danger often comes when we least expect it.  
Explanation: "When we least expect it" is the correct adverbial time clause meaning danger arrives at unexpected moments.

(e) The lady speaks as if she were an expert.  
Explanation: "As if" with an unreal or hypothetical idea takes the subjunctive ("were") to show she is not actually an expert.

Question #278 (ID: 481400)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) This is Bangladesh —.

(b) The people of Bangladesh are friendly though —.

(c) When anyone falls in danger, others —.

(d) We love and help one another as if —.

(e) We work seriously in order that Bangladesh —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) This is Bangladesh which is our motherland .

(b) The people of Bangladesh are friendly though they are not rich .

(c) When anyone falls in danger, others come forward to help him/her .

(d) We love and help one another as if we were brothers .

(e) We work seriously in order that Bangladesh can prosper day by day .

Explanation:
Explanation:
(a) The blank needs a relative clause of place introduced by "where" (e.g. "This is Bangladesh where I was born") because "Bangladesh" is a place.  
(b) "Though" shows contrast, so it should be followed by a contrasting fact or clause (e.g. "though many are poor" or "though not wealthy").  
(c) This is a general truth, so use the simple present with the plural subject "others" (e.g. "others help him/her").  
(d) "As if" makes a comparison and for an unreal or emphatic comparison we use the subjunctive/past form: "as if we were brothers."  
(e) "In order that" expresses purpose and is usually followed by "may/might" + verb (e.g. "in order that Bangladesh may prosper").

Question #279 (ID: 481401)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) He pretends as if —.

(b) It is high time —.

(c) Walk slowly lest —.

(d) — cannot succeed.

(e) Had I seen you before —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) He pretends as if he were mad .

(b) It is high time we did the task .

(c) Walk slowly lest you should/might fall down .

(d) Those who are idle , cannot succeed.

(e) Had I seen you before, I would have given you some money .

Explanation:
a After "as if" we use a past tense (or past perfect) to show something is unreal or contrary to fact, e.g. "He pretends as if he knew everything" — the past form "knew" shows the pretence, not reality.

b "It is high time" is followed by a past simple to express that something should happen now, e.g. "It is high time you went" — the past verb "went" functions like a subjunctive expressing present necessity.

c "Lest" introduces a negative purpose and takes a subjunctive or "should" form, e.g. "Walk slowly lest you fall" (or "lest you should fall") — it warns against an expected undesirable outcome.

d Use a negative pronoun with a positive auxiliary to avoid a double negative, e.g. "No one can succeed" (not "No one cannot succeed"); "cannot" pairs with an affirmative subject like "he" or "they."

e "Had I seen you before" uses inversion for the third conditional; it means "If I had seen you before, I would have told you," so the inverted "Had I..." replaces "If I had..." to show the unreal past condition.

Question #280 (ID: 481402)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Smoking is a habit which —.

(b) Many people go on smoking though —.

(c) —, we will suffer a lot.

(d) People can’t give up smoking easily because —.

(e) So attempts must be taken by us to —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Smoking is a habit which is harmful to health/causes fatal diseases .

(b) Many people go on smoking though they know its adverse effect/it is dangerous .

(c) If we do not give up smoking , we will suffer a lot.

(d) People cannot give up smoking easily because they become addicted to it .

(e) So attempts must be taken by us to avoid smoking so that we can keep fit .

Explanation:
(a) The correct completion is "is injurious to health" because the relative clause introduced by "which" should describe the habit; smoking damages lungs and causes serious diseases. 

(b) "Many people go on smoking though it is harmful/addictive" fits because despite knowing the harm, social pressures and addiction make them continue. 

(c) "If we smoke, we will suffer a lot" shows the direct consequence: continued smoking leads to health problems and suffering. 

(d) "People can’t give up smoking easily because it is addictive" is right since nicotine creates physical and psychological dependence that makes quitting hard. 

(e) "So attempts must be taken by us to discourage smoking / help people quit" is appropriate because prevention, awareness and support are needed to reduce smoking and its harm.

Question #281 (ID: 481403)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Acid rain is harmful because —.

(b) The wind was so strong that —.

(c) Had he been a little careful —.

(d) They were frightened when —.

(e) Take your umbrella lest —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Acid rain is harmful because it contains pollutants .

(b) The wind was so strong that it could blow off my hat .

(c) Had he been a little careful he could have avoided the accident .

(d) They were frightened when the earthquake had struck .

(e) Take your umbrella lest it should rain .

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক "'because' কারণ বোঝায়, তাই বাক্যের শেষ অংশে আঘাতের কারণ বলা উচিত; উদাহরণ: 'Acid rain is harmful because it damages plants, corrodes buildings and harms aquatic life.' এটি কারণ‑বর্ণনা দেয়, তাই সঠিক।  

খ "'so ... that' ফল‑প্রকাশ করে: প্রথম অংশে মাত্রা/পরিমাণ এবং পরে 'that' দিয়ে তার ফল বলা হয়; উদাহরণ: 'The wind was so strong that it blew the roof off.'  

গ "Had he been a little careful ..." হল অতীতের আনরিয়াল শর্ত (inversion of 'if he had...') যা অতীতের ভিন্ন ফলাফল ধরে; পূরণ হবে: '...he would not have made that mistake.'  

ঘ "They were frightened when ..."‑এ 'when' সময়/ঘটনা জানায় যা ভয়ের কারণ; উদাহরণ: 'They were frightened when they saw the snake.' এটি কারণ ও সময় সঠিকভাবে সংযুক্ত করে।  

ঙ "Take your umbrella lest ..."‑এ 'lest' নেগেটিভ উদ্দেশ্য বা সতর্কতা বোঝায় (মানে 'so that ... not'); সাধারণ পূরণ: 'Take your umbrella lest you get wet' বা পুরানো রীতি মতে 'lest you should get wet.'

Sub-Questions:

Question #282 (ID: 481404)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) He asked me —.

(b) — how it can be done.

(c) Hardly had he started for school —.

(d) He told me that —.

(e) — there is a way.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) He asked me where I went .

(b) She want to know how it can be done.

(c) Hardly had he started for school when the rain started .

(d) He told me that honesty is the best policy .

(e) Where there is a will , there is a way.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক He asked me where I was going. — প্রতিবেদিত প্রশ্নে প্রশ্নবোধক শব্দ (where) রাখা হয় কিন্তু বাক্যক্রম সাধারণ অর্থাৎ subject + verb হয় এবং tense অনুসারে পরিবর্তিত হয় (go → was going).

খ He showed me how it can be done. — 'how' দিয়ে শুরু হওয়া clause টি একধরণের object-clause, তাই 'how + subject + modal/verb' ক্রম বজায় থাকে এবং এটি কাজটি কীভাবে করা যায় তা বোঝায়।

গ Hardly had he started for school when it began to rain. — 'Hardly/Scarcely … when' конструкশনে inversion (Had he started) লাগে এবং এরপর সাধারণত 'when' দিয়ে দ্বিতীয় ঘটনা শুরু হয় (began to rain)।

ঘ He told me that he would come the next day. — সরাসরি বক্তব্য প্রতিবেদন করলে 'that' দিয়ে clause আসে এবং সময়/কাল backshift হয় (will → would, today → the next day)।

ঙ I wonder if there is a way. — প্রশ্নবোধক হ্যাঁ/না ধরনের ভাব প্রতিবেদন করতে 'if/whether' ব্যবহার করা হয় এবং বাক্যক্রম সরল থাকে (if + subject + verb)।

Question #283 (ID: 481405)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) We come to know about the happenings of home and abroad if

(b) People read newspaper lest

(c) Many students do not read newspaper regularly as

(d) Many people earn their living by

(e) I become happy when

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) We come to know about the happenings of home and abroad if we read newspaper .

(b) People read newspaper lest they should miss the latest news .

(c) Many students do not read newspaper regularly as they are busy with their study/they are not aware of the importance of reading newspaper .

(d) Many people earn their living by selling newspapers .

(e) I become happy when I get good news .

Explanation:
(a) if we read newspapers. Newspapers report important events at home and abroad, so reading them keeps us informed about current affairs.

(b) lest they remain ignorant. "Lest" means to prevent something, so people read newspapers to avoid being uninformed about important news.

(c) as they are too busy with studies or lack the habit. Many students prioritize academic work or have little time or interest, so they don’t read newspapers regularly.

(d) by working in the newspaper industry (as journalists, printers, vendors, etc.). The newspaper business provides various jobs—reporting, editing, printing and selling—that people depend on for income.

(e) when I read good news. Positive or favorable news gives pleasure and relief, so reading good news naturally makes one happy.

Question #284 (ID: 481406)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) 1971 is the year when —.

(b) Though Bangladesh has limited natural resources, —.

(c) — because he is not attentive to study.

(d) Be truthful if —.

(e) His silence proves that —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) 1971 is the year when Bangladesh became independent .

(b) Though Bangladesh has limited natural resources, these resources can help us make progress .

(c) He can't cut a good figure in the exam because he is not attentive to study.

(d) Be truthful if you want to be successful in life .

(e) His silence proves that he agrees to do this work .

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক 1971 হল সেই সাল যখন বাংলাদেশ স্বাধীনতা অর্জন করে; এটি ঐতিহাসিকভাবে সঠিক কারণ 1971 সালের স্বাধীনতা-যুদ্ধের মাধ্যমে দেশটি পাকিস্তান থেকে মুক্তি পায়।  

খ যদিও বাংলাদেশের প্রাকৃতিক সম্পদ সীমিত, তবু দেশের মানবসম্পদ (জনশক্তি), কৃষি ও উদ্যোগ তাকে উন্নয়নে সহায়তা করে; তাই সীমিত প্রাকৃতিক সম্পদের পরেও অগ্রগতি সম্ভব।  

গ সে ফেল করেছে কারণ সে পড়াশোনায় মনোযোগী নয়—এখানে 'because' একটি কারণ-ব্যাখ্যার শব্দ যা ফল (ফেল) ও কারণ (মনোযোগী না হওয়া) যোগ করে।  

ঘ সততা বজায় রাখো যদি তুমি বিশ্বাস বা সম্মান পেতে চাও; 'if' শর্ত বোঝায়—বিশ্বাস পাওয়ার শর্ত হিসেবে সত্য बोलাকে নির্দেশ করে।  

ঙ তার নীরবতা প্রমাণ করে যে সে সম্মত; সাধারণ বিবেচনায় নীরবতা অনেক সময় সম্মতি বোঝায় ("silence implies consent")।

Question #285 (ID: 481407)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Yesterday I could not get up from bed in time because

(b) As soon as I got up from bed —.

(c) Since I could not avail the bus, —.

(d) On the way to school. I walked fast lest —.

(e) If I reached late, —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Yesterday I could not get up from bed in time because I was ill/I went to bed late .

(b) As soon as I got up from bed, I went to the bathroom/I started to get ready for school .

(c) Since I could not avail the bus, I hired a taxi .

(d) On the way to school, I walked fast lest I should miss the class .

(e) If I reached late, my class teacher would punish me .

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক "because" একটি কারণ দেখায়, তাই বাক্যের প্রধান ক্রিয়ার সঙ্গে সময় মিল রেখে কারণটি অতীত কালেই দিতে হবে (উদাহরণ: "because my alarm didn't ring" বা "কারণ আমি বেশি ঘুমিয়ে ছিলাম")।

খ "As soon as" দুটি কাজের তাত্ক্ষণিক ক্রম প্রকাশ করে; তাই উভয় ক্রিয়াই সাধারণত অতীত কালেই থাকে (উদাহরণ: "As soon as I got up from bed, I brushed my teeth")।

গ "Since" কারণ নির্দেশ করে; কারণবাচক ক্লজের পরে ফলাফল দিতেই হবে এবং সময়一致 রাখতে উভয় ক্লজের কাল মিলতে হবে (উদাহরণ: "Since I could not avail the bus, I walked to school")।

ঘ "lest" নেতিবাচক উদ্দেশ্য প্রকাশ করে—কিছু ঘটাবার প্রতিরোধে—এবং পরে প্রায়শই subjunctive বা "should" আসে (উদাহরণ: "I walked fast lest I should be late")।

ঙ "If I reached late" একটি শর্তমূলক বাক্য শুরু করে; বাস্তব বা অভ্যাসজনিত গত প্রেক্ষাপটে ফলাফল দেখাতে প্রধান ক্লজে অতীতকাল বা "would/used to" ব্যবহার করা হয় (উদাহরণ: "If I reached late, the teacher would scold me" বা অভ্যাসে "If I reached late, the teacher used to scold me")।

Question #286 (ID: 481408)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) An educational institution is a seat of learning —.

(b) It should be a peaceful place where —.

(c) But now-a-days peaceful atmosphere is absent from educational institutions because —.

(d) The students who —.

(e) The sooner it can be controlled, the —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) An educational institution is a seat of learning, so we should be sincere enough to maintain its sanctity .

(b) It should be a peaceful place where the learners can carry on their studies uninterrupted .

(c) But nowadays peaceful atmosphere is absent from educational institutions because the students are engaged in creating an abnormal situation there .

(d) The students who are punctual, shine in life .

(e) The sooner it can be controlled, the better the situation will be .

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: (a) একটি শিক্ষাপ্রতিষ্ঠান শেখার কেন্দ্র কারণ এখানে জ্ঞান প্রদান ও চরিত্র গঠন হয়। (b) এটি শান্তিপূর্ণ হওয়া উচিত যাতে শিক্ষক ও ছাত্র মনোযোগ দিয়ে পড়াশোনা ও পাঠদান করতে পারে। (c) আজকাল রাজনৈতিক হস্তক্ষেপ, র্যাগিং ও অশাসন-অনুশীলনের কারণে শান্তিধারার অবনতিই মূল কারণ; (d) এই ধরনের অনুশাসিত বা সহিংস ছাত্ররা অন্যদের পড়াশোনা ব্যাহত করে। (e) এসব যত দ্রুত নিয়ন্ত্রণ করা যায়, তত দ্রুত শিক্ষা পরিবেশ স্বাভাবিক ও ফলপ্রসূ হবে।

Question #287 (ID: 481409)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Five years have passed since------.

(b) It is a matter of sorrow that------.

(c) I tried to write to you but------.

(d) In fact, we all are always------.

(e) We hope that we-----.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Five years have passed since we met last .

(b) It is a matter of sorrow that you do not utilize your time .

(c) I tried to write to you but failed due to my tight schedule .

(d) In fact, we all are always gifted with Almighty's blessings .

(e) We hope that we will succeed in the exam .

Explanation:
(a) "Five years have passed since I last saw him." — Present perfect ([math]have\ passed[/math]) is used to show time elapsed up to now, and "since" introduces the past point ("I last saw him").

(b) "It is a matter of sorrow that he died." — The structure "It is a matter of sorrow that + clause" introduces a regretful fact; the clause after "that" reports the sorrowful event in the appropriate tense.

(c) "I tried to write to you but I couldn't." — "Tried" (past) shows an attempt, and "but" contrasts it with the result; a negative like "couldn't" or "was unable to" completes the idea of failure.

(d) "In fact, we all are always learning." — "Are always" + present participle expresses a continued or habitual action; this structure emphasizes that learning is ongoing.

(e) "We hope that we will succeed." — "Hope" expresses a desire about the future, so it is natural to use "that" plus a future tense ("we will succeed") to state the expected outcome.

Question #288 (ID: 481410)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Many people cut trees —.

(b) Trees cause rainfall which —.

(c) If we cut trees at random, —.

(d) Trees supply oxygen —.

(e) Since trees help us in many ways —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Many people cut trees as they do not know their importance .

(b) Trees cause rainfall which is needed for our cultivation/is essential for our agriculture .

(c) If we cut trees at random, one day our country will turn into a desert/one day there will be no trees left .

(d) Trees supply oxygen which we take in.

(e) Since trees help us in many ways, we should plant more and more trees .

Explanation:
(a) Many people cut trees for timber, fuel and to clear land. This completion shows purpose — the sentence needs a phrase explaining why people cut trees.

(b) Trees cause rainfall which helps maintain soil moisture and supports agriculture. The relative clause introduced by "which" should describe the beneficial effect of that rainfall.

(c) If we cut trees at random, soil erosion and floods will increase. This is a cause–effect conditional: removing trees causes loss of root binding, so erosion and flooding follow.

(d) Trees supply oxygen essential for human and animal life. This states a factual result of photosynthesis, so the completion should name the life-supporting role of oxygen.

(e) Since trees help us in many ways, we must protect and plant more of them. The sentence gives a reason, so the natural completion is a conclusion or recommendation based on that reason.

Question #289 (ID: 481411)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) As a flower is a symbol of love, beauty and purity, it is —.

(b) There is hardly any person —.

(c) We can turn enemies into friends if we —.

(d) It is said that those who do not love flowers —.

(e) Many people cultivate flowers because —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) As flower is a symbol of love, beauty and purity, it is loved by all/everybody .

(b) There is hardly any person who does not like flowers/who hates flower .

(c) We can turn our enemies into friends if we present them flowers/offer flower/offer them flowers .

(d) It is said that those who do not love flowers, can kill anybody/can commit any crime/are capable of killing .

(e) Many people cultivate flowers because they earn their livedlihood/it is their earning source /(source of income)/it is profitable .

Explanation:
ক ফুল ভালোবাসা, সৌন্দর্য ও পবিত্রতার প্রতীক হওয়ায় মানুষের চোখে তা বিশেষ সুন্দর ও প্রশংসনীয়—তাই এটি সকলের কাছে আকর্ষণীয় বা প্রশংসিত।

খ প্রায় সবাই ফুল পছন্দ করে; তাই বলা হয় যে কমই এমন মানুষ আছে যিনি ফুল পছন্দ করেন না—এটি সাধারণ মানুষের স্বভাবগত রুচি নির্দেশ করে।

গ শত্রুকে বন্ধু করা যায় যদি আমরা সদয়তা, ক্ষমা বা মমত্ব প্রদর্শন করি; ভালো আচরণ অন্যের মন বদলে দিতে সাহায্য করে।

ঘ যারা ফুল পছন্দ করে না তাদের সম্পর্কে বলা হয় যে তাদের হৃদয়ে কোমলতা বা সৌন্দর্যের অনুভূতি কম—এটি ফুলপ্রতি অনুরাগকে মানবিক কোমলতার প্রতীক হিসেবে দেখায়।

ঙ অনেকেই ফুল চাষ করে কারণ ফুল পরিবেশ সুন্দর করে, খুশি দেয় এবং ব্যবসায়িক বা আয়-উৎস হিসেবে কার্যকর—এই কারণে ফুলের চাহিদা ও গুরুত্ব বেশি।

Question #290 (ID: 481412)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) If you do not waste time —.

(b) This is the boy —.

(c) — I were a child.

(d) United we stand, —.

(e) The boy is so weak in mathematics —.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) If you do not waste your time, you will shine in life .

(b) This is the boy who secured the first place in the exam .

(c) I wish I were a child.

(d) United we stand, divided we fall .

(e) The boy is so weak in mathematics that he can never pass in it in the exams .

Explanation:
(a) "If you do not waste time, you will succeed." — This is a first conditional: the if-clause uses the present simple and the main clause uses "will" to show a likely future result.

(b) "This is the boy who helped me." — Use "who" for people when the relative clause is the subject (he helped), so "who" correctly introduces the clause.

(c) "If only I were a child." — "If only" expresses a wish about an unreal present situation; the subjunctive "were" is used after wishes (not "was").

(d) "United we stand, divided we fall." — This is a fixed proverb showing contrast; "divided we fall" completes the balanced antithesis to "united we stand."

(e) "The boy is so weak in mathematics that he cannot solve the problem." — The "so... that" pattern links degree to result: his weakness is the cause and the inability to solve the problem is the result.

Question #291 (ID: 481413)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) We must work hard in order that —–.

(b) A man who —- cannot shine in life.

(c) It is hard labour that —-

(d) The idle cannot reach their target because —-

(e) —- unless you work hard.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) We must work hard in order that we can succeed in life .

(b) A man who wastes time in idleness , cannot shine in life.

(c) It is hard labour that helps a man to reach his goal .

(d) The idle cannot reach their target because they waste their valuable time .

(e) You will suffer in the long run unless you work hard.

Explanation:
(a) We must work hard in order that we may succeed.
Explanation: "In order that" expresses purpose and is followed by a clause showing the intended result; "may succeed" correctly shows the goal of working hard.

(b) A man who does not work hard cannot shine in life.
Explanation: The relative clause "who does not work hard" defines the kind of man, and the negative shows the consequence that he cannot succeed or "shine."

(c) It is hard labour that brings success.
Explanation: This cleft sentence ("It is ... that") emphasizes the cause; it shows that hard labour is the key factor producing success.

(d) The idle cannot reach their target because they do not work hard.
Explanation: "Because" gives the reason — idleness (not working hard) is the cause of failing to reach targets.

(e) Nothing can be achieved unless you work hard.
Explanation: "Unless" means "if not," so this conditional states that without hard work, achievement is impossible.

Question #292 (ID: 481414)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Yesterday I did not get up early from bed because, —–.

(b) As soon as I got up from bed, ——.

(c) As I could not hire a rickshaw, —–.

(d) On the way to school I walked fast lest —-.

(e) If I reached late, —-.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Yesterday I did not get up early from bed because I was ill/I went to bed late .

(b) As soon as I got up from bed, mother told me to take breakfast/I noticed that it was 9 o'clock/I saw that I was late to go to school .

(c) As I could not hire a rickshaw, I began to walk fast/I became awful .

(d) On the way to school I walked fast lest I should miss the class/I should miss an important class .

(e) If I reached late, I would be punished/I should miss an important class/I would miss the first period .

Explanation:
ক কারণ (because) ভাগের সাথে কারণ দেই, তাই একই কাল (অতীত) ব্যবহার করতে হবে — উদাহরণ: “because I was feeling unwell” বা “because I was very tired” যেন বাক্যটির বদ্দলটি ঘটনার সময়ের সাথে মিল থাকে। 

খ “As soon as” সময় নির্দেশ করে এবং সঙ্গে সঙ্গে ঘটা ক্রিয়ার কথা বলে, তাই সাধারণত সরাসরি অতীত কালের ক্রিয়া লাগে — উদাহরণ: “I brushed my teeth” বা “I had my breakfast.” 

গ এখানে “As I could not hire a rickshaw” কারণ দেখায়, ফলে ফলাফল শুদ্ধভাবে অতীতে বলা হবে, যেমন “I had to walk to school” বা “I walked to school.” 

ঘ “lest” মানে ‘ভয়ে যাতে না’ — এটি সাধারণত ‘should’ + মূল ক্রিয়া বা ‘may/might’ দিয়ে পাছার উদ্দেশ্য/ভয় বোঝায়; সঠিক: “lest I should be late” (অথবা “lest I be late”)। 

ঙ “If I reached late” হলে ফলাফল দুইভাবে লেখা যায়: যদি সাধারণ অতীত অভিজ্ঞতা বোঝাতে চান তবে ফলাফলও অতীতে রাখবেন (“my teacher scolded me”); যদি সম্ভাব্য পরিণতি বোঝাতে চান তবে শর্তাধীন ফলাফল gebruikt=”would” (“I would be punished”).

Question #293 (ID: 481415)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) United we stand, -------.

(b) It is high time we,------.

(c) Unless you are united,------.

(d) ------ know this wise saying?

(e) The story of the old man and his sons teaches us, -------.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) United we stand, divided we fall .

(b) It is high time we stopped quarrelling with each other/united/changed our lifestyle/food habit/manner/behaviour .

(c) Unless you are united, you will be destroyed by your enemics/you cannot be successful/cannot succeed/you will fail/you can't prosper in life .

(d) Do you/Who does not know this wise saying?

(c) The story of the old man and his sons teaches us that unity is strength/unity/to be united .

Explanation:
(a) United we stand, divided we fall.  
Explanation: This is a fixed proverb contrasting unity and disunity; it means people succeed when they are united and fail when they are divided.

(b) It is high time we left.  
Explanation: After "It is high time" English uses a past-tense verb (here "left") to express that something should happen immediately or is overdue.

(c) Unless you are united, you will fail.  
Explanation: "Unless" introduces the negative condition (if you are not united); the result clause states the consequence of that condition.

(d) Who does not know this wise saying?  
Explanation: This rhetorical question uses the negative form to imply that the saying is very well known; "Who doesn't know...?" is a common idiom.

(e) The story of the old man and his sons teaches us that unity is strength.  
Explanation: The tale shows that individual sticks are weak but together they are strong, so its moral is that unity brings strength.

Question #294 (ID: 481416)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) No sooner had I reached home than-------.

(b) He was so lazy that-------.

(c) It is health which-------.

(d) He succeeded though-------.

(e) As our elders love us,---------.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) No sooner had I reached home than it started raining .

(b) He was so lazy that he could not finish the job in time .

(c) It is health which is wealth .

(d) He succeeded though he did not work hard .

(e) As our elders love us, we should obey them .

Explanation:
(a) No sooner had I reached home than it began to rain.
Explanation: "No sooner ... than" shows that one event happened immediately after another and requires inversion (auxiliary before subject) in the first clause.

(b) He was so lazy that he did not finish his work.
Explanation: "So ... that" expresses a cause–result relationship: the adjective "lazy" is the cause and the clause after "that" gives the consequence.

(c) It is health which makes life worth living.
Explanation: This is a cleft/relative structure emphasizing "health"; "which" introduces the clause that describes the role or importance of health.

(d) He succeeded though he had little experience.
Explanation: "Though" introduces a concession meaning "in spite of"; it contrasts the unexpected success with the limiting condition.

(e) As our elders love us, we should respect them.
Explanation: "As" gives a reason (because), so the main clause expresses the appropriate response or consequence to that reason.

Question #295 (ID: 481417)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) ------- if he told me.

(b) The answer that he ------.

(c) Finishing the work,------.

(d) I saw my mother------.

(e) To walk in the morning------.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) would be present there if he told me.

(b) The answer that he gave me was not satisfactory .

(c) Finishing the work, I went to market .

(d) I saw my mother cooking food in the kitchen .

(e) To walk in the morning is good for health .

Explanation:
(a) "I would help him if he told me." — This is a second conditional: the if-clause uses past simple "told" to show a hypothetical situation, so the main clause uses "would" + base verb ("would help").

(b) "The answer that he gave." — The relative clause uses past simple "gave" because it refers to a completed action in the past.

(c) "Finishing the work, he went home." — A participle clause ("Finishing the work") shows an action done just before the main action; the subject of the participle is the same as the subject of the main clause ("he").

(d) "I saw my mother crossing the road." — After perception verbs you can use "object + -ing" to show an ongoing action; you can also say "I saw my mother cross the road" (bare infinitive) to mean you witnessed the whole action.

(e) "To walk in the morning is healthy." — An infinitive phrase acts as the subject here, so it takes a singular verb ("is") and expresses a general truth or habit.

Question #296 (ID: 481353)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Change the sentences according to directions given in the bracket:

(a) Simplicity is a great virtue. (Exclamatory)

(b) Everybody appreciates this quality. (Negative)

(c) It is one of the best qualities. (Positive)

(d) One should practise this virtue. (Passive)

(e) Very few men are as happy as a simple man. (Comparative)

(f) By practising simplicity one can earn people's favour. (Negative)

(g) A simple man leads a very carefree life. (Exclamatory)

(h) No other person among us is as happy as a simple man. (Superlative)

(i) Everybody should like simplicity. (Imperative)

(j) So, a simple life should be led by all. (Active)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Changing Sentences:

(a) What a virtue simplicity is! (সরলতা কী যে এক গুণ!)

(b) There is nobody but appreciates this quality. (এমন কেউ নেই যে এই গুণের প্রশংসা করে না।)

Or, There is nobody who does not appreciate this quality. (অথবা, এমন কেউ নেই যে এই গুণের প্রশংসা করে না।)

(c) Very few qualities are as good as it. (খুব কম গুণই এর মতো ভালো।)

(d) This virtue should be practised. (এই গুণের অনুশীলন করা উচিত।)

(e) A simple man is happier than most other men. (একজন সরল মানুষ অন্য অধিকাংশ মানুষের চেয়ে বেশি সুখী।)

(f) Without practising simplicity, none can earn people's favour. (সরলতার চর্চা না করে কেউই মানুষের অনুগ্রহ অর্জন করতে পারে না।)

(g) What a carefree life a simple man leads! (একজন সরল মানুষ কতই না দুশ্চিন্তামুক্ত জীবনযাপন করে।)

(h) A simple man is the happiest person among us. (একজন সরল মানুষ আমাদের মধ্যে সবচেয়ে সুখী ব্যক্তি।)

(i) Let everybody like simplicity. (সবাই সরলতা পছন্দ করুক।)

(j) So, all should lead a simple life. (তাই, সকলের উচিত সরল জীবনযাপন করা।)

Explanation:
(a) What a great virtue simplicity is!
Explanation: Exclamatory sentences use "What" (noun phrase + subject + verb) to express strong feeling; here the structure emphasizes the praise of simplicity.

(b) Nobody fails to appreciate this quality.
Explanation: To convert to a negative without changing the meaning, use "nobody fails to…" which keeps the original affirmative sense that all appreciate it.

(c) It is a very good quality.
Explanation: Changing from superlative ("one of the best") to the positive degree removes comparison; "very good" gives the plain positive form.

(d) This virtue should be practised.
Explanation: Passive voice with a modal uses "should be" + past participle, so the object ("this virtue") becomes the subject of the passive sentence.

(e) A simple man is happier than most men.
Explanation: Comparative degree uses "happier than" to compare two groups; this conveys the same idea as "very few men are as happy as…".

(f) By practising simplicity one cannot fail to earn people's favour.
Explanation: Using "cannot fail to" is a negative form that preserves the original meaning (that practising simplicity will certainly earn favour).

(g) What a very carefree life a simple man leads!
Explanation: Exclamatory form with "What" + noun phrase + subject + verb expresses surprise or strong feeling about the carefree life.

(h) A simple man is the happiest person among us.
Explanation: Superlative uses "the + adjective + noun" to show the highest degree of happiness within the group.

(i) Let everyone like simplicity.
Explanation: Imperative for a general command or wish uses "Let" + object (everyone) + base verb to address all persons.

(j) So, everyone should lead a simple life.
Explanation: Active voice makes "everyone" the subject performing the action; it changes "should be led by all" into the corresponding active form.

Question #297 (ID: 481354)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Bangladesh is a low-lying country. (Change it into Interrogative)

(b) Every year natural disasters visit us. (Change it into passive voice)

(c) Who does not know the consequence of Tsunami? (Change it into Assertive sentence)

(d) The recent flood was very devastating. (Change it into Exclamatory sentence) 

(e) Dhaka is the most risky city in the earthquake zone. (Change it into positive degree)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Isn't Bangladesh a low-lying country?

(b) We are visited by natural disasters every year.

(c) Everyone/Everybody knows the consequence of Tsunami.

Or, All know the consequence of Tsunami.

(d) How devastating the recent food was!

(e) No other city is as risky as Dhaka in the earthquake zone.

Or, No other city in the earthquake zone is as risky as Dhaka.

Explanation:
(a) "Is Bangladesh a low-lying country?"  
To form an interrogative in present simple, invert the auxiliary verb "is" and the subject "Bangladesh."

(b) "Every year we are visited by natural disasters."  
In passive voice the object "us" becomes the subject "we" and the active verb "visit" becomes "are visited" to match present simple tense.

(c) "Everyone knows the consequences of a tsunami."  
An assertive sentence states the idea directly; replace the interrogative "Who does not know..." with the universal affirmative "Everyone knows..."

(d) "How devastating the recent flood was!"  
For exclamation with an adjective use "How + adjective + subject + verb" to show strong feeling about how devastating the flood was.

(e) "Dhaka is a risky city in the earthquake zone."  
Change the superlative "the most risky" to the positive degree "risky"; the sentence then simply states the quality without comparison.

Question #298 (ID: 481355)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Computer is one of the greatest inventions of modern science. (Make it positive)

(b) In fact, it is a blessing of science. (Make it negative without changing the original meaning.)

(c) It has facilitated the world very greatly. (Make it exclamatory)

(d) Moreover, it has lessened our workloads. (Make it passive)

(e) So, we should use it in our everyday life. (Make it imperative)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Very few inventions of modern science are as great as computer.

(b) In fact, it is not a curse of science.

(c) How greatly it has facilitated the world!

(d) Moreover, our workloads have been lessened by it.

(e) So, let us use it in our everyday life.

Explanation:
ক The computer is one of the greatest inventions of modern science. Explanation: The sentence is already positive (affirmative); adding "The" makes it grammatically complete and natural.

খ In fact, it is not a curse of science. Explanation: A negative form using the antonym "curse" preserves the original positive meaning by denying the opposite.

গ How greatly it has facilitated the world! Explanation: An exclamatory sentence uses "How" + subject + verb to express strong feeling about the degree of facilitation.

ঘ Moreover, our workloads have been lessened by the computer. Explanation: In passive voice the object ("our workloads") becomes the subject and the verb changes to "have been lessened," with the agent introduced by "by."

ঙ Use it in your everyday life. Explanation: An imperative sentence gives a direct command; the subject "you" is omitted and the verb starts the sentence.

Question #299 (ID: 481356)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Very few conquerors of the world were so great as Taimur. (Superlative)

(b) The province of a powerful prince was once attacked by young Taimur. (Active)

(c) He captured a large village. (Passive)

(d) The army killed Taimur's all soldires. (Negative)

(e) He did not disguise himself as a rich traveller to survive. (Affirmative)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) Taimur was one of the greatest conquerors of the world.

(b) Once young Taimur attacked the provinces of a powerful prince.

(c) A large village was captured by him.

(d) The army did not leave Taimur's any soldiers.

Or, No soldier of Taimur could escape being killed by the army.

(e) He disguised himself as a poor traveler to survive.

Explanation:
(a) "Taimur was one of the greatest conquerors of the world." — এখানে অর্থটি বোঝাতে আমরা "one of the + plural superlative (greatest)" ব্যবহার করি, কারণ বাক্যটি বলে যে খুব কম জয়ী তার সমান।

(b) "Young Taimur once attacked the province of a powerful prince." — passive থেকে active তে রূপান্তর করতে করেছে যিনি কাজটি করেছেন (Taimur) তাকে subject করে verb‑টাইম একই রেখে বাক্য সাজানো হয়েছে।

(c) "A large village was captured by him." (বা "A large village was captured by Taimur.") — passive বানাতে object‑কে subject করা হয় এবং মূল verb কে past participle দিয়ে "was + past participle" ব্যবহার করা হয়।

(d) "The army did not kill all of Taimur's soldiers." — negative past simple গঠনের জন্য "did not" + base verb (kill) ব্যবহার করা হয়; এছাড়া "soldires" → "soldiers" এবং "all of" সঠিক ক্রমানুসারে বসানো হয়েছে।

(e) "He disguised himself as a rich traveller to survive." — affirmative তৈরি করতে "not" সরিয়ে দিয়েছেন এবং past simple form "disguised" ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।

Question #300 (ID: 481357)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) Only you can do the work. (Negative)

(b) No other friend is as great as books. (Superlative)

(c) The rose is a very nice flower. (Exclamatory)

(d) We should be patriots. (Imperative)

(e) He called it laurel. (Passive)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) None but you can do the work.

(b) Books are the greatest friend.

(c) What a nice flower the rose is!

(d) Let us be patriots.

(e) It was called laurel by him.

Explanation:
(a) Only you can do the work. (Negative)  
The word "only" excludes all others and gives the sentence a negative sense equivalent to "No one else can do the work," so it functions as a negative (restrictive) form.

(b) No other friend is as great as books. (Superlative)  
"No other" plus the comparison shows that none equals books, implying books are the greatest among friends, so the sentence conveys a superlative idea.

(c) The rose is a very nice flower. (Exclamatory)  
When expressed with strong feeling or an exclamation intonation (or recast as "What a very nice flower the rose is!"), the sentence becomes exclamatory because it emphasizes admiration.

(d) We should be patriots. (Imperative)  
Although it uses "should," the sentence gives a moral instruction or urging to a group (hortatory sense), so it functions as an imperative/advisory sentence.

(e) He called it laurel. (Passive)  
To make this passive you promote the object to subject: "It was called laurel by him." The sentence can therefore be expressed in passive voice by using "be" + past participle.
