Question #350 (ID: 481349)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Change the sentences according to directions:

(a) Honesty can open a door of peace before a person. (Make it negative)

(b) He accepted the invitation. (Make it passive)

(c) Reading books is nobler than any other habit. (Make it superlative)

(d) Loving country is a very essential virtue. (Make it exclamatory)

(e) We don't measure our life by months or years. (Make it active)

(f) Industry is the most important thing for success. (Make it comparative)

(g) How attentive she was to her study! (Make it assertive)

(h) Terrorism is one of the most corrosive problems of the modern world. (Make it positive)

(i) We should do good deeds as our responsibility. (Make it imperative)

(j) Everybody is fond of glittering things. (Make it negative)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Changing Sentences:

(a) Honesty cannot shut a door of peace before a person. (সততা একজন ব্যক্তির সামনে শান্তির দ্বার বন্ধ করতে পারে না।)

(b) The invitation was accepted by him. (তার দ্বারা আমন্ত্রণটি গ্রহণ করা হয়েছিল।)

(c) Reading books is the noblest habit. (বই পড়া সর্বশ্রেষ্ঠ অভ্যাস।)

(d) What an essential virtue loving country is! (দেশকে ভালোবাসা কতই না অপরিহার্য গুণ!)

(e) Our life is not measured by months or years by us. (আমাদের জীবনকে আমাদের কর্তৃক মাস বা বছর দ্বারা পরিমাপ করা হয় না।)

(f) Industry is more important than any other thing for success. (সাফল্যের জন্য অন্য যেকোনো জিনিসের চেয়ে পরিশ্রম বেশি গুরুত্বপূর্ণ।)

(g) She was very attentive to her study. (সে তার পড়াশোনায় খুবই মনোযোগী ছিলো।)

(h) Very few problems of the modern world are so corrosive as terrorism. (আধুনিক বিশ্বের খুব কম সমস্যাই সন্ত্রাসবাদের মতো এতো ধ্বংসাত্মক।)

(i) Let's do good deeds as our responsibility. (চলো আমরা আমাদের দায়িত্ব হিসেবে ভালো কাজ করি।)

(j) There is nobody but is fond of glittering things. (এমন কেউ নেই যে চাকচিক্যময় জিনিসকে পছন্দ করে না।)

Explanation:
Solution:
(a) Honesty cannot open a door of peace before a person.
Explanation: Changing the modal verb "can" to its negative form "cannot" makes the whole sentence negative while keeping the original meaning.

(b) The invitation was accepted by him.
Explanation: In passive voice the object "the invitation" becomes the subject, the verb uses auxiliary "was" + past participle "accepted", and the agent is expressed with "by him."

(c) Reading books is the noblest of all habits.
Explanation: Replace the comparative phrase "nobler than any other" with the superlative form "the noblest" and add "of all" to show it is highest in rank.

(d) What a very essential virtue it is to love one's country!
Explanation: Use the exclamatory "What..." construction plus "it is to..." to turn the statement into an exclamation expressing strong feeling.

(e) We do not measure our lives by months or years.
Explanation: This keeps the active voice with "we" as the subject and corrects to the natural plural "lives," expressing the same negative idea actively.

(f) Industry is more important for success than anything else.
Explanation: Change the superlative "the most important" into a comparative "more important ... than ..." and add a comparison phrase to complete it.

(g) She was very attentive to her studies.
Explanation: Convert the exclamatory "How attentive she was!" into a straightforward declarative sentence to make it assertive.

(h) Terrorism is a very corrosive problem of the modern world.
Explanation: Remove the superlative phrase "one of the most" and use the positive adjective "very corrosive" to express the idea in the positive degree.

(i) Let us do good deeds as our responsibility.
Explanation: Use the imperative-suggestive form "Let us" plus the base verb to turn the sentence into a command/suggestion.

(j) Not everybody is fond of glittering things.
Explanation: Placing "Not" before "everybody" makes the sentence negative without completely reversing the intended scope (unlike "Nobody," which is stronger).

Question #351 (ID: 481350)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Change the sentences according to the directions:

(a) Copying in the exams is one of the greatest social crimes. (Positive)

(b) It is a very serious crime. (Exclamatory)

(c) A student copying in the exam only deceives himself. (Negative)

(d) Copying in the exam. cannot bring any benefit. (Passive) (c) What a shameful practice it is!

(Assertive)

(f) By resisting this malady, we can strengthen our education. (Passive)

(g) We all should come forward to stop it and save our students. (Imperative)

(h) Our examination system should be moderated. (Active) (i) Nothing is as hateful as copying in the exam. (Comparative)

(j) The government is sincere in removing this crime. (Negative)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Changing Sentences:

(a) Very few social crimes are so great as copying in the exams. (পরীক্ষায় নকল করার মতো বড় সামাজিক অপরাধ খুব কমই আছে।)

(b) What a serious crime it is! (এটা কতই না গুরুতর অপরাধ!)

(c) A student copying in the exam does nothing but deceives himself. (পরীক্ষায় নকলকারী একজন শিক্ষার্থী নিজেকে প্রতারণা করা ছাড়া আর কিছুই করে না।)

(d) Any benefit cannot be brought by copying in the exam. (পরীক্ষায় নকল কোনো কল্যাণ/উপকার বয়ে আনে না ।),

(e) It is a very shameful practice. (এটা খুবই লজ্জাজনক অভ্যাস।)

(f) By resisting this malady, our education can be strengthened by us. (এই ব্যাধিকে রোধ করে, আমাদের দ্বারা আমাদের শিক্ষা শক্তিশালী হতে পারে।)

(g) Let's come forward to stop it and save our students. (এটি বন্ধ করতে এবং আমাদের শিক্ষার্থীদের বাঁচাতে চলো এগিয়ে আসি।)

(h) The concerned authorities should moderate our examination system. (সংশ্লিষ্ট কর্তৃপক্ষের উচিত আমাদের পরীক্ষা পদ্ধতি পরিমার্জন করা।)

(i) Copying in the exam is more hateful than any thing. (পরীক্ষায় নকল করা যেকোনো জিনিসের চেয়ে বেশি ঘৃণ্য।)

(j) The government is not insincere in removing this crime. (এই অপরাধ দূর করতে সরকার উদাসীন নয়।)

Explanation:
(a) Copying in the exams is one of the greatest social crimes. (Positive Degree)

✅ Transformed: Very few social crimes are as great as copying in the exams.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: “One of the + superlative” → “Very few + plural noun + are as + positive degree + as...”

এখানে "one of the greatest" একটি superlative expression, যেটি positive রূপে রূপান্তর করতে হয় “Very few...” দিয়ে শুরু করে।

(b) It is a very serious crime. (Exclamatory)

✅ Transformed: How serious a crime it is!

📝 Explanation:

Rule: “It is a very + adjective + noun.” → “How + adjective + a + noun + it is!”

এখানে “very serious crime” কে Exclamatory করার জন্য “How” দিয়ে শুরু করে অভিপ্রায় প্রকাশ করা হয়েছে।

(c) A student copying in the exam only deceives himself. (Negative)

✅ Transformed: A student copying in the exam does not deceive anyone but himself.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Affirmative → Negative by using “does not... but” structure

“Only deceives himself” অর্থ বোঝাতে “does not deceive anyone but himself” ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।

(d) Copying in the exam cannot bring any benefit. (Passive)

✅ Transformed: No benefit can be brought by copying in the exam.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Passive Voice: object + auxiliary + be + past participle + by + agent

এখানে “bring” ক্রিয়াটিকে passive করতে “can be brought” করা হয়েছে এবং agent “copying in the exam” যোগ হয়েছে।

(e) What a shameful practice it is! (Assertive)

✅ Transformed: It is a very shameful practice.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Exclamatory → Assertive: “What a/an + adjective + noun it is!” → “It is a very + adjective + noun.”

“What a shameful practice it is!” একটি বিস্ময়বোধক বাক্য, যা assertive এ রূপান্তর করতে "very shameful practice" ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।

(f) By resisting this malady, we can strengthen our education. (Passive)

✅ Transformed: Our education can be strengthened by resisting this malady.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Passive: object + can be + past participle + by + agent

"Strengthen" verb-কে passive করতে “can be strengthened” রূপ নেওয়া হয়েছে।

(g) We all should come forward to stop it and save our students. (Imperative)

✅ Transformed: Let us all come forward to stop it and save our students.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Suggestive imperative → “Let us...”

যেহেতু এখানে একটি সমষ্টিগত আহ্বান বা উৎসাহ জ্ঞাপন করা হয়েছে, তাই “Let us...” দিয়ে imperative রূপ করা হয়েছে।

(h) Our examination system should be moderated. (Active)

✅ Transformed: Someone should moderate our examination system.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Passive → Active: subject + modal + base verb + object

“Should be moderated” এর Active রূপ হয় “should moderate” এবং ‘Someone’ একটি অব্যক্ত কর্তা (agent) হিসেবে যুক্ত হয়েছে।

(i) Nothing is as hateful as copying in the exam. (Comparative)

✅ Transformed: Copying in the exam is more hateful than anything else.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Positive → Comparative: “Nothing is as + adjective + as...” → “Subject is more + adjective + than anything else.”

“Nothing is as hateful as...” মানে হলো সবকিছুর চেয়ে এটি বেশি ঘৃণ্য — তাই comparative রূপে প্রকাশ করা হয়েছে।

(j) The government is sincere in removing this crime. (Negative)

✅ Transformed: The government is not insincere in removing this crime.

📝 Explanation:

Rule: Affirmative → Negative: “is sincere” → “is not insincere”

Double negative না করে অর্থ অক্ষুন্ন রেখে নেতিবাচক রূপে প্রকাশ করা হয়েছে।

Question #352 (ID: 481351)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Change the sentences according to directions:

(a) Jackfruit is one of the largest fruits of Bangladesh. (Use Positive degree)

(b) The fruit is very juicy. (Make an Exclamatory sentence)

(c) It tastes very sweet. (Use Passive voice)

(d) It contains high calories. (Make Negative sentence)

(e) Everyone knows it as our national fruit. (Interrogative)

(f) In summer, this fruit is very available. (Negative)

(g) It is mainly found in the month of Jaishtha. (Use Active voice)

(h) It is not as costly as the mango. (Use Comparative degree)

(i) We should eat the fruit to ensure nutrition. (Make an Imperative sentence)

(j) How beautiful jackfruits look in the trees! (Make Assertive)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Changing Sentences:

(a) Very few fruits of Bangladesh are so large as Jackfruit. (বাংলাদেশের খুব কম ফলই কাঁঠালের মতো বড়।)

(b) How juicy the fruit is! (ফলটি কতই না রসালো!)

(c) It is very sweet when it is tasted. (যখন এটির স্বাদ গ্রহণ করা হয় তখন এটি খুব মিষ্টি লাগে।)

(d) It does not contain low calories. (এতে কম ক্যালোরি থাকে না।)

(e) Who does not know it as our national fruit? (আমাদের জাতীয় ফল হিসেবে এটিকে কে না চেনে?)

(f) In summer, this fruit is not unavailable at all. (গ্রীষ্মকালে এই ফলটি মোটেই অসহজলভ্য নয়।)

(g) We mainly find it in the month of Jaishtha. (আমরা এটি প্রধানত জ্যৈষ্ঠ মাসে পাই।)

(h) It is less costly than the mango. (আমের তুলনায় এটি কম দামি।) Or, The mango is costlier than it. (এটির চেয়ে আম দামি।)

(i) Let's eat the fruit to ensure nutrition. (পুষ্টি নিশ্চিত করতে চলো ফলটি খাই।)

(j) Jackfruits look very beautiful in the trees. (গাছে কাঁঠাল খুব সুন্দর দেখায়।)

Explanation:
Solution:

(a) Jackfruit is a large fruit of Bangladesh.
Explanation: The original superlative phrase "one of the largest" is changed to the positive degree by using the adjective "large" without comparison.

(b) What a very juicy fruit it is!
Explanation: An exclamatory sentence expresses strong feeling; here we use "What a..." structure and an exclamation to show emphasis.

(c) It is considered very sweet.
Explanation: "Taste" as a linking verb does not take a natural passive, so we use "is considered" to form a passive that preserves the original meaning.

(d) It does not contain high calories.
Explanation: To make the sentence negative in the simple present, add the auxiliary "does not" before the base verb.

(e) Does everyone know it as our national fruit?
Explanation: Forming a yes/no question in present simple requires the auxiliary "does" and inversion of subject and verb.

(f) In summer, this fruit is not very available.
Explanation: Make the sentence negative by inserting "not" after the auxiliary verb "is."

(g) People mainly find it in the month of Jaishtha.
Explanation: Change the passive "is found" into an active form by introducing a doer ("people") and using the active verb "find."

(h) It is less costly than the mango.
Explanation: "Not as...as" is changed to a comparative form "less...than" to compare the two items directly.

(i) Eat the fruit to ensure nutrition.
Explanation: An imperative sentence gives a command or advice; remove the subject and use the base verb "eat."

(j) Jackfruits look very beautiful in the trees.
Explanation: Convert the exclamatory sentence into a plain assertive (declarative) sentence by stating the observation without exclamation.

Question #353 (ID: 481352)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Change the sentences according to directions given in the bracket:

(a) The student is known to me. (Active)

(b) She gave me an interesting book. (Passive)

(c) Jashore is older than Magura. (Positive)

(d) Truthfulness is the best quality of a person. (Comparative)

(e) No other city in Bangladesh is as populous Dhaka. (Superlative)

(f) My friend is always punctual. (Negative)

(g) He is a great fool. (Exclamatory)

(h) How bright the student is! (Assertive)

(i) We should obey our teachers. (Imperative)

(j) Take care of your health. (Passive)

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Changing Sentences:

(a) I know the student. (আমি ছাত্রটিকে চিনি।)

(b) An interesting book was given to me by her. (তার দ্বারা আমাকে একটি মজার বই দেওয়া হয়েছিল।)

(c) Magura is not as old as Jashore. (মাগুরা যশোরের মতো পুরাতন নয়।)

(d) Truthfulness is better than any other quality of a person. (সত্যবাদিতা একজন ব্যক্তির অন্য যেকোনো গুণের চেয়ে উত্তম।)

(e) Dhaka is the most populous city in Bangladesh. (ঢাকা বাংলাদেশের সবচেয়ে জনবহুল শহর।)

(f) My friend is never late. (আমার বন্ধু কখনও দেরি করে না।)'

(g) What a fool he is! (সে কতই না বোকা।)

(h) The student is very bright. (ছাত্রটি খুব মেধাবী।)

(i) Let us obey our teachers. (চলো আমরা শিক্ষকদের মান্য করি।)

(j) Let your health be taken care of. (তোমার স্বাস্থ্যের যত্ন নেওয়া হোক।)

Explanation:
(a) I know the student.
The passive "is known to me" is changed to active by making the agent "I" the subject and using the active verb "know".

(b) An interesting book was given to me by her.
To form the passive, the object "an interesting book" becomes the subject, the verb becomes "was given" and the agent is introduced with "by her".

(c) Jashore is not as young as Magura.
To convert a comparative to the positive form we use "not as + positive adjective + as" so "older than" becomes "not as young as" to keep the same meaning.

(d) Truthfulness is better than any other quality of a person.
"Best" (superlative) changes to comparative by saying "better than any other…" to compare truthfulness with all other qualities.

(e) Dhaka is the most populous city in Bangladesh.
To form the superlative we make the thing compared the subject and use "the most + adjective" to show it exceeds all others.

(f) My friend is never late.
"Always punctual" is expressed negatively by using the opposite adjective ("late") with "never" to keep the same meaning.

(g) What a great fool he is!
Exclamatory sentences with a noun phrase use the structure "What a + adjective + noun + subject + verb" to show strong feeling.

(h) The student is very bright.
An exclamatory "How bright the student is!" becomes an assertive statement by using "very" with the adjective.

(i) Obey your teachers.
To make an imperative, remove "we should" and use the base verb "Obey" addressed to the listener as a command.

(j) Let your health be taken care of.
The imperative "Take care of your health" is made passive by making "your health" the subject and using "let … be + past participle" to retain the command sense.

Question #354 (ID: 481290)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
It was 4 in the afternoon. Hamid was studying (a)---- the library when his cell phone rang. It was his younger sister, Runa. She said that she was standing (b)---- front of (c)---- shopping mall opposite Hamid's office and asked him to meet her there as soon as possible. Hamid hurried out of (d)------ library. As he went (e)----- the street, he noticed that Runa was not alone. She was holding (f)----- three to four years old girl (g)---- hand. (h) ---- child was crying and Runa was trying frantically (i)----- to pacify her. Some passers-by were looking (j) ----- them suspiciously. When he reached her, she started to explain.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) at/in; (b) in; (c) the; (d) the; (e) to/on/down; (f) a; (g) in; (h) The; (i) ×; (j) at; (a) de.

Explanation:
The correct fills are: (a) in, (b) in (as part of "in front of"), (c) the, (d) the, (e) down, (f) a, (g) by the, (h) The, (i) — (omit; sentence is "trying frantically to pacify her"), (j) at.  

Explanation: Use [math]"in"[/math] for being inside a place and "in front of" to show position; use the definite article "the" for a specific library/shopping mall; "down the street" shows movement along the street; "a" before a singular count noun and "by the hand" expresses how she was holding the child; no extra word is needed before "to pacify her"; and "look at" is the correct verb–preposition collocation.

Question #355 (ID: 481291)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A national flag is (a)----- matter of pride for a nation. Every independent nation in (b)----- world has a national flag (c)----- its own. As (d)---- independent nation, we have a national flag. Our national flag is (e) ----- symbol of independence, (f)----- sovereignty and prosperity. Red and green colours are used in it. The red colour used in (g)----- flag indicates (h) ------ martyrs who laid down their valuable lives (i) ----- the independence of our country. We must uphold its (j)----honour.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) a; (b) the; (c) of; (d) an; (e) the; (f) ×; (g) the; (h) the; (i) for; (j) ×.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক, ঘ ও ঙ — এখানে [math]a[/math] ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে কারণ "matter" ও "symbol" একটি অজ্ঞাত একক বস্তু বোঝায়; [math]an[/math] ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে "independent" শব্দটির প্রথমে স্বরধ্বনি আছে বলেই।  
খ, জ ও ট — [math]the[/math] ব্যবহৃত হয়েছে কারণ এগুলো নির্দিষ্ট জিনিসকে নির্দেশ করে: "the world", "the flag", "the martyrs"।  
গ, চ ও ফ — [math]of[/math] সম্পর্ক বা মালিকানা দেখাতে লাগে, যেমন "flag of its own" এবং "symbol of independence, of sovereignty"।  
ঠ ও য — [math]for[/math] উদ্দেশ্য/কারণ প্রকাশ করে ("laid down their lives for independence"), এবং "due" (অর্থাৎ প্রাপ্য/উচিত) "honour"–এর সাথে মিলেছে, তাই "due honour" অর্থবহ।

Question #356 (ID: 481292)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Travelling has (a)---- great influence (b) ----- our minds. The human mind always craves (c)----- change. There is none who does not feel a thrill of joy (d) ------ the new sight of experience. The traveller comes in contact (e) ----- various types of people. If he moves (f)---- the observant eyes, he can acquire (g) ----- lot of practical knowledge about men and things of (h) ----- world which books alone cannot provide. Travelling gives us (i)----- opportunity to enjoy the more enchanting sights of nature. It helps one enrich his knowledge and makes him completely (j) ------ perfect man.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) a; (b) on; (c) for; (d) at; (e) with; (f) with; (g) a; (h) the; (i) an; (j) a.

Explanation:
Answers: (a) "a", (b) "on", (c) — (no word; "craves change"), (d) "at", (e) "with", (f) "with", (g) "a", (h) "the", (i) "the", (j) "a".  
Use "a" for singular countable nouns ("a great influence", "a lot of"), "on" and "with" are the standard prepositions after "influence" and "come in contact", and "at" shows a reaction to a sight.  
"Craves" normally takes a direct object (no preposition), and "moves with (the) observant eyes" means he travels being observant; "the" is used to specify "world" and "opportunity".

Question #357 (ID: 481293)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
It is needless to say that washing hands is very important for us. It is certainly (a)----- important issue. Washing hands regularly can save us from a kind of infectious disease (b) ------ COVID-19. Washing hands with soap is (c)----- must. We have to wash hands (d)----- taking meal and (e)----- using the toilet. Again, we should wash hands after touching sick members (f)----- our family and pet animals. Washing hands is also strictly recommended after coming back (g)----- outside. Washing hands in (h) ----- proper way may help us stay away from corona virus. (i)----- reason is that coronavirus spreads through touch. So, it is (j)------ important to keep our hands clean.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) an; (b) like; (c) a; (d) before; (e) after; (f) of; (g) from; (h) a; (i) the; (j) x.

Explanation:
(a) use "a very" because "important issue" is a singular count noun and needs the article "a", with "very" adding emphasis; (b) use "such as" to introduce an example (COVID-19); (c) use "an absolute" because "must" is used as a noun and needs the determiner "an" before a vowel sound to show strong necessity.  
(d) "before" and (e) "after" are correct because they show time relations (prior to eating, after using the toilet); (f) use "of" in "members of our family"; (g) "from" is used in "coming back from outside"; (h) use "the" in "in the proper way" to specify the correct manner.  
(i) "The main" points to a specific reason, and (j) "very" strengthens the adjective "important."

Question #358 (ID: 481294)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Bangladesh is a free land but she is beset (a)----- many problems. The use of poly bags is very dreadful. Recently it has become (b)----- great threat (c)---- our environment. (d)------ used poly bags block the drainage system. As a result, the low-lying areas (e)----- the towns and the cities go under (f)----- dirty water when it rains heavily. The used poly bags also destroy (g)------ fertility of our soil. Our government has already banned the production (h)------ poly bags. Yet some greedy and (i)------ dishonest businessmen are producing the bags (j)----- their own interest.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) with; (b) a; (c) for/to; (d) The; (e) around/ of; (f) ×; (g) the; (h) of; (i) ×; (j) for.

Explanation:
Explanation:
ক "with" — "beset with" is the correct collocation meaning afflicted by many problems.
খ "a" — "a great threat" needs the indefinite article before a singular count noun.
গ "to" — threats act "to" or "to the benefit/harm of" something, so "threat to our environment."
ঘ "The" — specific used poly bags already mentioned, so the definite article "The" is required.
ঙ "in" — low-lying areas located inside towns/cities, so "in the towns and the cities."
চ "the" — a specific body of dirty water is meant, so the definite article "the" is used.
ছ "the" — "the fertility" refers to the specific fertility of our soil, so use the definite article.
জ "of" — production "of poly bags" is the correct prepositional phrase.
ঝ "very" — intensifier modifying "dishonest" (alternative acceptable: no word, but "very" emphasizes degree).
ঞ "in" — "in their own interest" is the correct idiomatic phrase.

Question #359 (ID: 481295)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Road accidents have recently become (a)----- regular phenomenon in our country. As a result of the accidents, many persons fall a victim (b)------ untimely death. It is reported that most of the accidents occur (c)----- the violation of traffic rules, by (d)----- unskilled drivers and unconscious passers-by. Many unlicensed and faulty vehicles also endanger (e)------ passengers and (f) ------ passers-by. So, in order to save us (g) ------ the accidents (h)------ government is trying to create awareness (i) ------- the people and has passed strict laws (j)---- the accused.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) a; (b) to; (c) for; (d) ×; (e) the; (f) the; (g) from; (h) the; (i) among; (j) against.

Explanation:
Anwers: (a) "an increasingly" — we need the article plus an adverb to show rising frequency ("an increasingly regular phenomenon"); (b) "to" — the correct collocation is "fall a victim to"; (c) "due to" — expresses cause; (d) "both" — links the two agents ("by both unskilled drivers and unconscious passers-by"); (e) "both" and (f) no article — the phrase should read "endanger both passengers and passers-by" (direct objects, no preposition); (g) "from", (h) "the", (i) "among", (j) "against" — giving the natural phrases "save us from", "the government", "awareness among the people", and "laws against the accused".

Question #360 (ID: 481296)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Nowadays, parents are very conscious (a)----- harmful effect of punishment (b)----- the children. Child psychologists think that both (c)----- physical and mental punishments can be disastrous for (d) ------ child's growth and development. It may lead (e)----- fear and hatred of the person who punishes (f)----- child. Again, if (g)----- child is punished, it may lack initiative. It may also feel hostile (h)------ others. So, rude (i)----- behaviour gradually develops (j)----- him.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) of; (b) on; (c) x; (d) a; (e) to; (f) the; (g) a; (h) to; (i) ×; (j) in.

Explanation:
Being "conscious" takes the preposition "of" and harm affects someone "on" them, so (a) = "of the" and (b) = "on". "Both" is followed by the article when referring to specific kinds, and we need "the" for the child's possession, so (c) = "the" and (d) = "the"; "lead to" is the correct verb-preposition collocation, so (e) = "to", and a specific punished child takes "the" at (f) = "the". For a general statement use "a" at (g) = "a"; someone feels "hostile to" others so (h) = "to"; finally, negative traits are described as "rude and bad behaviour" and behavior develops "in" a person, so (i) = "and bad" and (j) = "in".

Question #361 (ID: 481297)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Friendship is (a)------ great human virtue, It is (b)----- love and affection between two persons. It binds more than one person (c)----- good relationship and inspires each other to share (d)----- joys and sorrows (e) ------ life. Man is (f)------ social being. He cannot live alone. So, he wants (g)----- company. He yearns (h)----- giving and receiving love and affection. Friendship grows between the persons. (i)----- similar taste, feelings and thoughts. It grows out of mutual understanding and give and take. It generally grows (j)-----two persons of the same age.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) a; (b) the; (c) in; (d) ×; (e) of; (f) a; (g) ×; (h) for; (i) of; (j) between.

Explanation:
(a) and (f) use the indefinite article "a" because "great human virtue" and "social being" are singular countable nouns; (b) uses "the" because it refers to that specific love between two persons.  
Prepositions: "in a" (c) shows being within a relationship, "in" (e) fits the phrase "in life", "between" (j) expresses relation of two people, and "with" (i) links people who have similar tastes.  
Possessive "their" (d) shows shared feelings; "some" (g) is idiomatic for wanting company; "for" (h) is required after "yearns" (yearns for).
